<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">Official state car</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image">
<div style="width:52px"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg"><img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" height="39" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" width="50"/></a></div>
</td>
<td class="mbox-text"><span class="mbox-text-span">This article <b>needs additional citations for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verification</a></b>. <span class="hide-when-compact">Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit">improve this article</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.</span> <small><i>(January 2013)</i></small> <small class="hide-when-compact"><i>(<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></span></td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>An <b>official state car</b> is a car used by a government to transport its <a href="/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">head of state</a> or <a href="/wiki/Head_of_government" title="Head of government">head of government</a> in an official capacity, which may also be used occasionally to transport other members of the government or visiting dignitaries from other countries. A few countries bring their own official state car for <a href="/wiki/State_visit" title="State visit">state visits</a> to other countries, for instance the USA, Russia and sometimes the UK. It also may serve as an automotive symbol of the head of state and their country. Part of the criteria for an official state car is to have adequate security, capability and stateliness for its duty. A <a href="/wiki/Limousine" title="Limousine">limousine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Executive_car" title="Executive car">executive car</a> or <a href="/wiki/Sport_utility_vehicle" title="Sport utility vehicle">sport utility vehicle</a> is usually selected.</p>
<p>Due to the high security risk for the passengers, these vehicles are often heavily secured and protected. <a href="/wiki/Armored_car_(VIP)" title="Armored car (VIP)">Vehicles may be armored</a> by the manufacturer or an after-market specialist. (In this article the term "armored car" invariably means a reinforced civilian vehicle, not the <a href="/wiki/Armored_car_(military)" title="Armored car (military)">military vehicle</a> often so named.) When carrying an important passenger, state vehicles may be surrounded by a <a href="/wiki/Motorcade" title="Motorcade">motorcade</a> consisting of police or military personnel. The vehicle's driver might also be from the law enforcement or military pool; the driver of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Presidential_State_Car_(United_States)" title="Presidential State Car (United States)">United States Presidential State Car</a> is an experienced agent from the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secret_Service" title="United States Secret Service">Secret Service</a>, <a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">Russian President</a>'s driver is a ranking officer of the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Protective_Service_(Russia)" title="Federal Protective Service (Russia)">Federal Protective Service</a>, and the British Prime Minister is driven by a <a href="/wiki/Protection_Command#Specialist_Protection" title="Protection Command">Specialist Protection</a> officer from the Metropolitan Police Service.</p>
<p>For <a href="/wiki/State_visit" title="State visit">state visits</a> and international conferences, the host country usually supplies the ground transportation and security personnel. However, a few countries transport their official state cars to the destination.</p>
<p>In countries that have indigenous automobile manufacturers, the government will usually commission one of the national automakers to provide a state car, or allow several to provide cars for an official state fleet. It is considered an honour for a car manufacturer to be selected to provide a state car for their respective country and a demonstration of the confidence of a government in their national industry.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Autoblog.com_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-Autoblog.com-1">[1]</a></sup> For example, the President of the United States currently uses a <a href="/wiki/Cadillac" title="Cadillac">Cadillac</a> with special undisclosed security features commissioned by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_government" title="United States government">United States government</a> and built by <a href="/wiki/General_Motors" title="General Motors">General Motors</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Motor_Company" title="Lincoln Motor Company">Lincoln</a>, manufactured by <a href="/wiki/Ford_Motor_Company" title="Ford Motor Company">Ford Motor Company</a> and <a href="/wiki/Chrysler" title="Chrysler">Chrysler</a> vehicles having been used in the past, representing the three major American manufacturers. <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet</a> leaders used the custom-built limousines by the <a href="/wiki/ZiL" title="ZiL">ZiL</a> company, and though the Russian Presidents have switched to the <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a> due to Zil's decline after the <a href="/wiki/Dissolution_of_the_Soviet_Union" title="Dissolution of the Soviet Union">Dissolution of the Soviet Union</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a> has commissioned a new official state car from the national automotive establishment to be delivered by 2020. The <a href="/wiki/Emperor_of_Japan" title="Emperor of Japan">Emperor of Japan</a> uses a <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Century" title="Toyota Century">Toyota Century</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Italy" title="Prime Minister of Italy">Prime Minister of Italy</a> uses a <a href="/wiki/Maserati" title="Maserati">Maserati</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Malaysia" title="Prime Minister of Malaysia">Prime Minister of Malaysia</a> uses a <a href="/wiki/Proton_Perdana_(first_generation)" title="Proton Perdana (first generation)">Proton Perdana</a>, the <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Czech_Republic" title="President of the Czech Republic">President of the Czech Republic</a> rides a <a href="/wiki/%C5%A0koda_Auto" title="Škoda Auto">Škoda</a> <a href="/wiki/%C5%A0koda_Superb" title="Škoda Superb">Superb</a>, and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_monarch" title="British monarch">British monarch</a> uses a <a href="/wiki/Bentley" title="Bentley">Bentley</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Autoblog.com_1-1"><a href="#cite_note-Autoblog.com-1">[1]</a></sup> Members of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_Royal_Family" title="British Royal Family">British Royal Family</a> are driven in Jaguars, though other makes may be used in other <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_realm" title="Commonwealth realm">Commonwealth realms</a>. The <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President of France</a> can choose from cars manufactured by <a href="/wiki/Renault" title="Renault">Renault</a> or <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/PSA_Peugeot_Citro%C3%ABn" title="PSA Peugeot Citroën">PSA Peugeot Citroën</a>, and all major German manufacturers (<a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz" title="Mercedes-Benz">Mercedes-Benz</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW" title="BMW">BMW</a> and <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Group" title="Volkswagen Group">Volkswagen Group</a>) are represented in Germany's pool of vehicles available for use by state officials.</p>
<p>For countries without major indigenous manufacturers, an official state car may be purchased from a suitable manufacturer in a nation with strong economic and diplomatic ties. Canada exclusively uses state cars manufactured by the <a href="/wiki/Big_Three_(automobile_manufacturers)" title="Big Three (automobile manufacturers)">Detroit Three</a>, many of which are made in Canadian factories, with the United States and American car manufacturers having a historically strong relationship with Canada. The Canadian government also holds shares in General Motors and Chrysler following their restructuring in the economic downturn of 2008.</p>
<p>In some cases state cars may bear standard number plates; in others special or no plates are used.</p>
<p>The following information lists some state cars and their users of sovereign states and other territories; the list is likely to be out of date in some cases as incumbents and cars change.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Afghanistan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Afghanistan" title="President of Afghanistan">President of Afghanistan</a> travels in a convoy of armored <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Land_Cruiser#J200_.282007.E2.80.93present.29" title="Toyota Land Cruiser">Toyota Land Cruiser J200s</a> without registration plates.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Argentina">Argentina</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Argentina">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Presidential_car_(Argentina)" title="Presidential car (Argentina)">Presidential car (Argentina)</a></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Argentina" title="President of Argentina">President of Argentina</a> use a armored Mercedes-Benz Vito.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Australia">Australia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Australia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Official_convoy_Op_Catalyst_Welcome_Home_Parade.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2448" data-file-width="3264" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Official_convoy_Op_Catalyst_Welcome_Home_Parade.JPG/220px-Official_convoy_Op_Catalyst_Welcome_Home_Parade.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Official_convoy_Op_Catalyst_Welcome_Home_Parade.JPG/330px-Official_convoy_Op_Catalyst_Welcome_Home_Parade.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Official_convoy_Op_Catalyst_Welcome_Home_Parade.JPG/440px-Official_convoy_Op_Catalyst_Welcome_Home_Parade.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Official_convoy_Op_Catalyst_Welcome_Home_Parade.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A motorcade transporting senior members of the official party to an event in Canberra in November 2009. The black car at the left with the numberplate ADF1 carried the Chief of the Defence Force, the white car behind it with the numberplate C1 carried the Prime Minister and the black car second from the right carried the Governor General</div>
</div>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Governor-General_of_Australia">Governor-General of Australia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Governor-General of Australia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Governor-General_of_Australia" title="Governor-General of Australia">Governor-General of Australia</a> travels in a <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_VI" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom VI">Rolls-Royce Phantom VI</a> limousine for ceremonial occasions, such as the <a href="/wiki/State_Opening_of_Parliament" title="State Opening of Parliament">State Opening of Parliament</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> He more commonly uses a white ballistic and bullet-proof armoured BMW 7 series when on official business. The official cars of the Governor-General fly the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_the_Governor-General_of_Australia" title="Flag of the Governor-General of Australia">Flag of the Governor-General of Australia</a> and display <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Edward%27s_Crown" title="St. Edward's Crown">St. Edward's Crown</a> instead of number plates. A similar arrangement is used for the Governors of the six states. When the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Queen_of_Australia" title="Queen of Australia">Queen</a> is in Australia, the <a href="/wiki/Queen%27s_Personal_Australian_Flag" title="Queen's Personal Australian Flag">Queen's Personal Australian Flag</a> is flown on the car in which she is travelling. During the Queen's 2011 visit to Australia, the Queen and the <a href="/wiki/Prince_Philip,_Duke_of_Edinburgh" title="Prince Philip, Duke of Edinburgh">Duke of Edinburgh</a> were driven in a <a href="/wiki/Range_Rover" title="Range Rover">Range Rover</a> Vogue.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Prime_Minister">Prime Minister</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Prime Minister">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Prime_Ministerial_Limousine_(Australia)" title="Prime Ministerial Limousine (Australia)">Prime Ministerial Limousine (Australia)</a></div>
<p>The official state car of the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Australia" title="Prime Minister of Australia">Prime Minister of Australia</a> is a white ballistic and bullet-proof armoured <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_7-Series" title="BMW 7-Series">BMW 7-Series</a>, supported at all times by an armoured BMW X5. Prior to 2013, vehicles in the Prime Ministerial fleet were white <a href="/wiki/Ford_Territory" title="Ford Territory">Ford Territory</a> and Holden Caprice models.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> The Prime Ministerial vehicle is also escorted by police vehicles from state and federal authorities. The Prime Minister's car bears the number plate "C1" (meaning "Commonwealth 1") and a centrally mounted <a href="/wiki/List_of_Australian_flags" title="List of Australian flags">Australian flag</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> The Prime Ministerial car fleet operates as part of COMCAR, a division of the Australian Government's Department of Finance.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<p>In 2013, <a href="/wiki/BMW" title="BMW">BMW</a> was selected to provide a fleet of <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series_(F01)" title="BMW 7 Series (F01)">7-Series High Security</a> vehicles as part of a tender to replace the ageing armoured Holden Caprice fleet that formerly transported the Australian Prime Minister. The <a href="/wiki/Commercial_off-the-shelf" title="Commercial off-the-shelf">off-the-shelf</a> replacements offer greater protection and better value for money.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> A <a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems" title="BAE Systems">BAE</a> and GM-Holden <a href="/wiki/Consortium" title="Consortium">Consortium</a> also bid for the contract.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Austria">Austria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Austria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Senior government figures in Austria use <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a> models.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Azerbaijan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>President of <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan" title="Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> <a href="/wiki/Ilham_Aliyev" title="Ilham Aliyev">Ilham Aliyev</a> travels in an armored <a href="/wiki/Maybach_57_and_62" title="Maybach 57 and 62">Maybach 62</a> limousine.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> Sometimes he uses a heavy armored, custom-built <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W221#S_600_Guard_Pullman_.282008-.29" title="Mercedes-Benz W221">Mercedes-Benz W221 S600 Guard Pullman</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Bangladesh">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Prime Minister of Bangladesh travels in an armored BMW E65 7 series. Also used is Mercedes G class SUV.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Belgium">Belgium</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Belgium">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Belgian King, <a href="/wiki/Philippe_of_Belgium" title="Philippe of Belgium">Philippe</a>, uses a Mercedes Benz S600 or a BMW 7-Class mostly with the number plate, '1', because he is the commander in chief of the army. For the inauguration a <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_600" title="Mercedes-Benz 600">Mercedes-Benz 600</a> Landaulette was used. All royal family members drive cars with only numbers. The Prime Minister of Belgium, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charles_Michel_(politician)" title="Charles Michel (politician)">Charles Michel</a>, uses an Audi A6. Federal government officials drive cars with number plates starting with an "A" followed by one to three numbers. Regional government officials drive cars with number plates starting with an "E" followed by one to three numbers. Members of parliament and the senate drive cars with number plates starting with an "P" followed three numbers. For personal use, <a href="/wiki/Queen_Paola_of_Belgium" title="Queen Paola of Belgium">Queen Paola of Belgium</a> drives a <a href="/wiki/Fiat_500" title="Fiat 500">Fiat 500</a> with diplomatic plates. <a href="/wiki/Prince_Laurent_of_Belgium" title="Prince Laurent of Belgium">Prince Laurent of Belgium</a> is famous for his speed driving and his fast cars. There is also a <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_600" title="Mercedes-Benz 600">Mercedes-Benz 600</a> in the royal garage. The late <a href="/wiki/Baudouin_of_Belgium" title="Baudouin of Belgium">Baudouin of Belgium</a> ordered in the ’70s an armored <a href="/wiki/De_Tomaso_Deauville" title="De Tomaso Deauville">De Tomaso Deauville</a>. He had also an <a href="/wiki/Aston_Martin_DB2/4" title="Aston Martin DB2/4">Aston Martin DB2/4</a>. For their marriage in 1960, Baudouin and Fabiola used a 1955 <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_Series_62" title="Cadillac Series 62">Cadillac Series 62</a> Convertible, with a bulletproof bubble-top.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Bhutan">Bhutan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Bhutan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/King_of_Bhutan" title="King of Bhutan">King of Bhutan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jigme_Singye_Wangchuck" title="Jigme Singye Wangchuck">Jigme Singye Wangchuck</a>, drove a <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Land_Cruiser" title="Toyota Land Cruiser">Toyota Land Cruiser J100</a> when travelling around the kingdom. The present King of Bhutan is driven in a Range Rover and Mini Cooper.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Bolivia">Bolivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Bolivia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Bolivia" title="President of Bolivia">President of Bolivia</a> is driven in an armoured <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS" title="Lexus LS">Lexus LS 460</a>L<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> and escorted by four <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Land_Cruiser" title="Toyota Land Cruiser">Toyota Land Cruisers</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Brazil">Brazil</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Brazil">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Presidential_State_Car_(Brazil)" title="Presidential State Car (Brazil)">Presidential State Car (Brazil)</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:President_Lula_at_Independence_Day_commemorations_(2007).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1772" data-file-width="3543" height="110" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/President_Lula_at_Independence_Day_commemorations_%282007%29.jpg/220px-President_Lula_at_Independence_Day_commemorations_%282007%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/President_Lula_at_Independence_Day_commemorations_%282007%29.jpg/330px-President_Lula_at_Independence_Day_commemorations_%282007%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/President_Lula_at_Independence_Day_commemorations_%282007%29.jpg/440px-President_Lula_at_Independence_Day_commemorations_%282007%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:President_Lula_at_Independence_Day_commemorations_(2007).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Brazilian President <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/Presidential_State_Car_(Brazil)#Presidential_State_Car" title="Presidential State Car (Brazil)">presidential Rolls Royce</a>, during the 2007 <a href="/wiki/Independence_Day_(Brazil)" title="Independence Day (Brazil)">Independence Day</a> military parade.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The ceremonial state car of the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">President of Brazil</a> is a 1952 <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Silver_Wraith" title="Rolls-Royce Silver Wraith">Rolls-Royce Silver Wraith</a>, reserved exclusively for Independence Day commemorations, state visits and the <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_presidential_inauguration" title="Brazilian presidential inauguration">presidential inauguration</a>. The current <a href="/wiki/Presidential_State_Car_(Brazil)" title="Presidential State Car (Brazil)">official state car</a> used by the president for regular transportation is a 2011-model armored version of the <a href="/wiki/Ford_Fusion_Hybrid" title="Ford Fusion Hybrid">Ford Fusion Hybrid</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> The car is also used as escort car for the presidential motorcade. The Fusion was first used on 17 June 2008 when it replaced a 2004 <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Omega" title="Chevrolet Omega">Chevrolet Omega</a>.</p>
<p>In February 2012 the Brazilian government bought 12 Canadian-built <a href="/wiki/Ford_Edge" title="Ford Edge">Ford Edge</a> models, 10 of which armored, for the use of President <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">Dilma Rousseff</a> and her security team.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></p>
<p>The federal government's most important officials (President, Ministers, Magistrates, etc.) use yellow-green brass plates adorned with the <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_Brazil" title="Coat of arms of Brazil">coat of arms of Brazil</a> and their titles engraved on them (e.g., President of the Republic, President of the Senate, Defense Minister, Supreme Court President, etc.).</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Brunei">Brunei</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Brunei">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The ceremonial state car of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sultan_of_Brunei" title="Sultan of Brunei">Sultan of Brunei</a> is a 1992 state landaulette <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_VI" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom VI">Rolls-Royce Phantom VI</a>. On non-ceremonial occasions, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sultan_of_Brunei" title="Sultan of Brunei">Sultan of Brunei</a> personally drives a black <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_M-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz M-Class">Mercedes-Benz M-Class</a> W163 ML55 AMG, usually escorted by either a Secret Service <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E39" title="BMW E39">BMW E39</a> 540i or a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E61" title="BMW E61">BMW E61</a> 545i, and a few <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LX" title="Lexus LX">Lexus LX</a>470. Recently, his Majesty drives around in black Brabus G700. On other occasions he drives a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maybach_62" title="Maybach 62">Maybach 62</a>. The Sultan and his brother Prince <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jefri_Bolkiah" title="Jefri Bolkiah">Jefri Bolkiah</a> owns several thousand luxury and exotic cars, one of the largest collections in the world.</p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Queen_Saleha_of_Brunei" title="Queen Saleha of Brunei">Queen Saleha of Brunei</a> usually driven around in 2012 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rolls_Royce_Phantom" title="Rolls Royce Phantom">Rolls Royce Phantom</a> Series II.</p>
<p>The member of the Royal Family are usually escorted by a Secret Service escort <a href="/wiki/Volvo_S80" title="Volvo S80">Volvo S80</a> V8 models, or <a href="/wiki/Mitsubishi_380" title="Mitsubishi 380">Mitsubishi 380</a>.</p>
<p>The Cabinet Ministers of Brunei and visiting foreign dignitaries are driven in a black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_W221" title="Mercedes Benz W221">Mercedes Benz W221</a> S350L, while other senior ranking officials are driven in a black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_W211" title="Mercedes Benz W211">Mercedes Benz W211</a> E280.</p>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sultan_of_Brunei" title="Sultan of Brunei">Sultan of Brunei</a> drives <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_G-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz G-Class">Mercedes-Benz G-Class</a> the 2009 Facelifted G55 AMG instead of W163 ML55 AMG.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Bulgaria">Bulgaria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Bulgaria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The cars of the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Bulgaria" title="President of Bulgaria">President of Bulgaria</a> include <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S600" title="Mercedes-Benz S600">Mercedes-Benz S600</a> and <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a> and <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a>. The Prime Minister is being driven in a Toyota Land Cruiser, he very often drives it himself with the security guards sitting in the back of the car. The Prime Minister also is being driven in black <a href="/wiki/BMW_X5" title="BMW X5">BMW X5</a>. The pilot cars are usually <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ford" title="Ford">Ford</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota" title="Toyota">Toyota</a> or <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a> and <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a>. As on 18 December, the Prime minister and the President of Bulgaria are being transported in top class Mercedes S600 Guard, 517 hp.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Cambodia">Cambodia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Cambodia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Royal King of Cambodia <a href="/wiki/Norodom_Sihamoni" title="Norodom Sihamoni">Norodom Sihamoni</a> is driven in a black <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_600" title="Mercedes-Benz 600">Mercedes-Benz 600</a> with the logo of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Royal_Standard_of_the_King_of_Cambodia" title="Royal Standard of the King of Cambodia">Royal Standard of the King of Cambodia</a> behind. His Majesty has owned two black Mercedes-Benz 600s and also a black <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Land_Cruiser" title="Toyota Land Cruiser">Land Cruiser 100</a>.</p>
<p>The Prime Minister of Kingdom of Cambodia has owned more than 4 Mercedes-Benz guard cars and more than 5 <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Suburban" title="Chevrolet Suburban">Chevrolet Suburbans</a> in his houses. He also has had a black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S600" title="Mercedes-Benz S600">Mercedes-Benz S600</a> (W221) Carat Duchatelet bullet proof with plate number <code>2Z-9999</code> and another black Mercedes-Benz S600 (V221) with plate number <code>2AA-9999</code> and two gold Mercedes-Benz S600 (W220)s.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Canada">Canada</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Canada">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Royal_and_viceroyal_transport_in_Canada" title="Royal and viceroyal transport in Canada">Royal and viceroyal transport in Canada</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Motorcade_Winnipeg_Queen_Elizabeth_II.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="506" data-file-width="675" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Motorcade_Winnipeg_Queen_Elizabeth_II.jpg/220px-Motorcade_Winnipeg_Queen_Elizabeth_II.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Motorcade_Winnipeg_Queen_Elizabeth_II.jpg/330px-Motorcade_Winnipeg_Queen_Elizabeth_II.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Motorcade_Winnipeg_Queen_Elizabeth_II.jpg/440px-Motorcade_Winnipeg_Queen_Elizabeth_II.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Motorcade_Winnipeg_Queen_Elizabeth_II.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The motorcade of <a href="/wiki/Title_and_style_of_the_Canadian_monarch" title="Title and style of the Canadian monarch">Queen</a> <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">Elizabeth II</a> passing through <a href="/wiki/Winnipeg" title="Winnipeg">Winnipeg</a>; the sovereign's car (second in line) is a claret coloured <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Town_Car" title="Lincoln Town Car">Lincoln Town Car</a> bearing her <a href="/wiki/Royal_standards_of_Canada" title="Royal standards of Canada">personal standard for Canada</a>, with a licence plate showing a gold St. Edward's Crown on a red field</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Monarchy_of_Canada" title="Monarchy of Canada">Monarch of Canada</a> and <a href="/wiki/Governor_General_of_Canada" title="Governor General of Canada">Governor General of Canada</a> are driven in a <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Town_Car" title="Lincoln Town Car">Lincoln Town Car</a> or a <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_MKS" title="Lincoln MKS">Lincoln MKS</a> bearing the flag of either office on the right hand fender. The sovereign's car bears a licence plate showing a gold <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Edward%27s_Crown" title="St. Edward's Crown">St. Edward's Crown</a> on a red field, while the governor general's car bears a plate with the <a href="/wiki/Crest_(heraldry)" title="Crest (heraldry)">crest</a> of the Royal <a href="/wiki/Arms_of_Canada" title="Arms of Canada">Arms of Canada</a> (similar to the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_the_Governor_General_of_Canada" title="Flag of the Governor General of Canada">Flag of the Governor General of Canada</a>) or standard auto plates of the province of Ontario with flags of the governor general on the front hood. The governor general also has a Cadillac DTS stretch limousine at his/her disposal. A <a href="/wiki/Ford_Flex" title="Ford Flex">Ford Flex</a> is also in the Goveror General's fleet.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Canada" title="Prime Minister of Canada">Prime Minister of Canada</a> is driven in a motorcade of five cars or more. The motorcade is adjusted for certain public events, as seen fit by the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police" title="Royal Canadian Mounted Police">Royal Canadian Mounted Police</a>. The prime minister usually rides in an armoured long-wheelbase <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_DTS" title="Cadillac DTS">Cadillac DTS</a> or <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Suburban" title="Chevrolet Suburban">Chevrolet Suburban</a>, but has also been seen arriving at various events in a <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Sienna" title="Toyota Sienna">Toyota Sienna</a> minivan when travelling with members of his family. The prime minister is also eligible to use the governor general's Cadillac stretch limousine at various times. The prime minister's car bears standard Ontario car plates. His or her motorcade is usually led by a <a href="/wiki/Chrysler_300" title="Chrysler 300">Chrysler 300</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dodge_Charger" title="Dodge Charger">Dodge Charger</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Mercury_Grand_Marquis" title="Mercury Grand Marquis">Mercury Grand Marquis</a>.</p>
<p>Certain ministers and officials are driven in Chrysler 300 sedans. There is also a <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Tahoe" title="Chevrolet Tahoe">Chevrolet Tahoe</a> hybrid for official transportation.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Chile">Chile</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Chile">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The official presidential vehicle in Chile is a 1966 black <a href="/wiki/Ford_Galaxie" title="Ford Galaxie">Ford Galaxie</a> XL Convertible, given as a gift by the queen Elizabeth II on her visit to Chile. It is used only for official ceremonies celebrating national days on May 21, September 18 and September 19. It has a normal license plate (EL-2801).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Fordgalaxie.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1944" data-file-width="2592" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Fordgalaxie.JPG/220px-Fordgalaxie.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Fordgalaxie.JPG/330px-Fordgalaxie.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Fordgalaxie.JPG/440px-Fordgalaxie.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Fordgalaxie.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Chilean presidential car ready to go to the <a href="/wiki/National_Congress_of_Chile" title="National Congress of Chile">National Congress of Chile</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>For daily transport the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Chile" title="President of Chile">president</a> was previously driven in a <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Town_Car" title="Lincoln Town Car">Lincoln Town Car</a>, but President <a href="/wiki/Michelle_Bachelet" title="Michelle Bachelet">Michelle Bachelet</a> used a 2008-model <a href="/wiki/Peugeot_607" title="Peugeot 607">Peugeot 607</a> saloon. Her motorcade was often seen driving 2006 <a href="/wiki/Audi_A4" title="Audi A4">Audi A4</a> and <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">A6s</a>. Various 2007 Dodge Durangos also compose the presidential motorcade.</p>
<p>The newly elected president <a href="/wiki/Sebasti%C3%A1n_Pi%C3%B1era" title="Sebastián Piñera">Sebastián Piñera</a> was arrived at the Presidential Palace in a brand new 2010 BMW 760Li <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=BMW_F03&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="BMW F03 (page does not exist)">F03</a> (armored). Various Audi Q7's, BMW 5 series, Audi's A6 were seen driving along with him.</p>
<p>In May, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lexus_LS_600" title="Lexus LS 600">Lexus LS 600h</a>, was chosen by Piñera as the official presidential vehicle.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="China">China</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: China">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Before the production of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hongqi_(automobile)" title="Hongqi (automobile)">Hongqi</a>, Chinese leaders uses various foreign luxury cars. For example, Chairman <a href="/wiki/Mao_Zedong" title="Mao Zedong">Mao Zedong</a> used a bullet-proofed ZIL-115 donated from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stalin" title="Stalin">Stalin</a>, while Premier <a href="/wiki/Zhou_Enlai" title="Zhou Enlai">Zhou Enlai</a> used a GAZ-12 ZIM, later a ZIL-115 and Foreign Minister <a href="/wiki/Chen_Yi_(marshal)" title="Chen Yi (marshal)">Chen Yi</a> used a Mercedes-Benz 600 Pullman before Hongqi introduced its most famous CA770 into production. Since 1960s Chinese leaders have traditionally used limousines produced under the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FAW_Hongqi" title="FAW Hongqi">Hongqi</a> brand for official events. Before the new Hongqi HQE (official name L9) was introduced, the Chinese leaders used special version of CA770 limousine to review the troops in National Days. During former paramount leader <a href="/wiki/Hu_Jintao" title="Hu Jintao">Hu Jintao</a>'s review of troops on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/60th_Anniversary_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="60th Anniversary of the People's Republic of China">National Day</a> in 2009, he was seen in a <a href="/wiki/Hongqi_HQE" title="Hongqi HQE">Hongqi HQE</a> Limousine. The HQE is powered by an aluminium <a href="/wiki/V12_engine" title="V12 engine">V12</a> cylinder engine of Chinese design (designation CA12VG), with a displacement of 6.0 liters and producing 370 kW (470 hp) at 5600 rpm and 550 N m (405 lb·ft) of torque at 4400 rpm. It is bulletproof, completely hand built and comes with run flat tyres.</p>
<p>Started from early 90s, Chinese leaders have switched to using minibuses, such as the <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Coaster" title="Toyota Coaster">Toyota Coaster</a>, for short-distance trips.</p>
<p>When visiting a foreign country, Chinese leaders generally use vehicles supplied by the host country. This custom began to change in November 2014, when <a href="/wiki/Xi_Jinping" title="Xi Jinping">Xi Jinping</a>, <a href="/wiki/General_Secretary_of_the_Communist_Party_of_China" title="General Secretary of the Communist Party of China">General Secretary of the Communist Party</a>, used his own <a href="/wiki/Hongqi_L5" title="Hongqi L5">Hongqi L5</a> limousine on a state visit to New Zealand.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cctv2014_16-0"><a href="#cite_note-cctv2014-16">[16]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup> Chinese premiers continue to use cars supplied by the host country.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Colombia">Colombia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Colombia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Presidencia_de_Colombia.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="418" data-file-width="1123" height="82" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Presidencia_de_Colombia.jpg/220px-Presidencia_de_Colombia.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Presidencia_de_Colombia.jpg/330px-Presidencia_de_Colombia.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Presidencia_de_Colombia.jpg/440px-Presidencia_de_Colombia.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Presidencia_de_Colombia.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Colombian presidential motorcade</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Since 1991, the Colombian Presidential vehicles have usually been <a href="/wiki/BMW" title="BMW">BMWs</a>. In 2006, the Presidential fleet included four armoured <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_7-Series" title="BMW 7-Series">BMW 7-Series</a> and several units of Toyota Land Cruiser 100, whose level of armour is a state secret. These <a href="/wiki/BMW" title="BMW">BMWs</a> and Toyotas are equipped with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/GPS" title="GPS">GPS</a> and runflat tires. The motorcade is made up of 3 BMWs plus 5 Toyota 100s all armored plus a Prado armored level IIIA for Police Escort and an ambulance and no less than 8 motorcycles. All the vehicles have presidential tags.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Costa_Rica">Costa Rica</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Costa Rica">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_Costa_Rica" title="President of Costa Rica">President of Costa Rica</a>, Luis Guillermo Solís, as well his Vice-Presidents, Helio Fallas and Ana Helena Chacon, use grey or black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Toyota_Prado" title="Toyota Prado">Toyota Prado Land Cruisers</a> as their official state cars.</p>
<p>Other Ministers use similar cars.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Croatia">Croatia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Croatia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/President_of_Croatia" title="President of Croatia">President of Croatia</a> is driven in an armored Black <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup> and escorted by a selection of marked and unmarked BMW and Audi models driven by the members of the <a href="/wiki/Security_and_Intelligence_Agency" title="Security and Intelligence Agency">Croatian Secret Service</a>. President occasionally uses <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Passat" title="Volkswagen Passat">Volkswagen Passat</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_E-Class_(W212)" title="Mercedes-Benz E-Class (W212)">Mercedes-Benz E250</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-slobodnadalmacija1_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-slobodnadalmacija1-19">[19]</a></sup> These vehicles are part of the vehicle fleet of the <a href="/wiki/Honor_Guard_Battalion_(Croatia)" title="Honor Guard Battalion (Croatia)">Honor Guard Battalion</a>.</p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Croatia" title="Prime Minister of Croatia">Prime Minister of Croatia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Speaker_of_the_Croatian_Parliament" title="Speaker of the Croatian Parliament">Speaker of the Croatian Parliament</a> are like President driven in an armored Black <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a> with an escort, while Government Ministers use <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a> and <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-slobodnadalmacija1_19-1"><a href="#cite_note-slobodnadalmacija1-19">[19]</a></sup> These vehicles are part of the vehicle fleet of <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_the_Interior_(Croatia)" title="Ministry of the Interior (Croatia)">Ministry of the Interior</a>'s Department of Protection of Protected Persons.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Czech_Republic">Czech Republic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Czech Republic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The current president of <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech Republic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Milo%C5%A1_Zeman" title="Miloš Zeman">Miloš Zeman</a>, uses the Czech-made <a href="/wiki/%C5%A0koda_Superb" title="Škoda Superb">Škoda Superb</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Denmark">Denmark</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Denmark">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/Margrethe_II_of_Denmark" title="Margrethe II of Denmark">Queen Margrethe II</a> uses a 1958 Rolls-Royce Silver Wraith seven-seater (LGLW 25 body no. 10181), commonly referred to as <a href="/wiki/Royal_Danish_Ceremonial_Car_%22Store_Krone%22" title='Royal Danish Ceremonial Car "Store Krone"'>Store Krone (Great Crown)</a>. It was purchased by her father, <a href="/wiki/Frederick_IX_of_Denmark" title="Frederick IX of Denmark">Frederick IX of Denmark</a>, as new. The coachbuilder and seller was <a href="/wiki/Hooper_(coachbuilder)" title="Hooper (coachbuilder)">Hooper &amp; Co. (Coachbuilder)</a> Ltd, 54 St James Street, <a href="/wiki/Piccadilly" title="Piccadilly">Piccadilly</a>, London SW1.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup></p>
<p>In addition she uses several lesser cars for more common occasions. Noteworthy are Krone (Crown) 1, 2 and 5, which are all <a href="/wiki/Daimler_DS420" title="Daimler DS420">Daimler DS420</a> eight-seater limousines made in 1970, 1989 (purchased in 1994 with 1500 km on the clock) and 1986. There was also a <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Arnage" title="Bentley Arnage">Bentley Arnage</a> which has been replaced by a <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Mulsanne_(2010)" title="Bentley Mulsanne (2010)">Bentley Mulsanne</a> in 2012. The name Krone with a number, like Krone 121,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup> refers to the license plate used when carrying members of the <a href="/wiki/Danish_Royal_Family" title="Danish Royal Family">Danish Royal Family</a> inside Denmark.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup></p>
<p>The Queen is also using a hybrid limousine : the <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS_(XF40)" title="Lexus LS (XF40)">Lexus LS 600h L</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup> In Juli 2016 the queen and prince-consort used a stretched <a href="/wiki/Volvo_S80" title="Volvo S80">Volvo S80</a> by Nillson. Crown Prince Frederik uses a full electric <a href="/wiki/Tesla_Model_S" title="Tesla Model S">Tesla Model S</a> since the summer of 2013.</p>
<p>The current <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Denmark" title="Prime Minister of Denmark">Prime Minister of Denmark</a> uses an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Audi_A8L" title="Audi A8L">Audi A8 L</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ritzau_25-0"><a href="#cite_note-Ritzau-25">[25]</a></sup> The former one was driven in an armored <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a>. The ministers in the Danish government drive different kinds of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/VW_Phaeton" title="VW Phaeton">VW Phaeton</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a>, <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a>, <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a> and different <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ritzau_25-1"><a href="#cite_note-Ritzau-25">[25]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Dominican_Republic">Dominican Republic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Dominican Republic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The President of the <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">Dominican Republic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Danilo_Medina" title="Danilo Medina">Danilo Medina</a> actually uses a black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Toyota_Land_Cruiser_200" title="Toyota Land Cruiser 200">Toyota Land Cruiser 200</a> and a black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lexus_LX_570" title="Lexus LX 570">Lexus LX 570</a>, which can be seen normally with the 0–1 plate (Presidential Plate) and it's mostly chosen by the government for its reliability and bulletproofs armor, a black <a href="/wiki/Ford_Expedition" title="Ford Expedition">Ford Expedition</a> which was used during his campaign and is now being used as a security car and back up, a black <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a> used the inaugural parade, only used to go to events in or near the <a href="/wiki/Distrito_Nacional" title="Distrito Nacional">Distrito Nacional</a>, <a href="/wiki/Santo_Domingo" title="Santo Domingo">Santo Domingo</a>. All of the cars have been modified with bullet-proof tires and bullet-proof windows. The Presidential Plate will be changed to the car that the president will use for the day. The Escorts teams uses blacks <a href="/wiki/Toyota_4Runner" title="Toyota 4Runner">Toyota 4Runner</a> fourth and fifth generation, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Fortuner" title="Toyota Fortuner">Toyota Fortuner</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Land_Cruiser_Prado" title="Toyota Land Cruiser Prado">Toyota Land Cruiser Prado</a> J120 and the J150 on the motorcade.</p>
<p>Since 2013, the fleet of official state vehicles for the Governor of the state or province were changed from first generation <a href="/wiki/Nissan_X-Trail" title="Nissan X-Trail">Nissan X-Trail</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nissan_Frontier" title="Nissan Frontier">Nissan Frontier</a> D22 for new 2014 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mitsubishi_Montero" title="Mitsubishi Montero">Mitsubishi Montero</a> fourth generation. They also could use their own personal vehicles.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="East_Germany">East Germany</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: East Germany">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The former <a href="/wiki/East_Germany" title="East Germany">East Germany</a> manufactured the <a href="/wiki/Trabant" title="Trabant">Trabant</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wartburg_(car)" title="Wartburg (car)">Wartburg</a>, both deemed unsuitable for state car usage. The leaders of the country used Russian-made cars and Swedish <a href="/wiki/Volvo" title="Volvo">Volvo</a> models, while the <a href="/wiki/Socialist_Unity_Party_of_Germany" title="Socialist Unity Party of Germany">Communist Party</a> General Secretary, <a href="/wiki/Erich_Honecker" title="Erich Honecker">Erich Honecker</a>, used a fleet of stretched <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Citroen_CX" title="Citroen CX">Citroen CX</a> and <a href="/wiki/Volvo_700_Series" title="Volvo 700 Series">Volvo 700 Series</a> models.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ecuador">Ecuador</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Ecuador">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The presidential state car in <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a> is an armored <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Town_Car" title="Lincoln Town Car">Lincoln Town Car</a> purchased by president <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lucio_Gutierrez" title="Lucio Gutierrez">Lucio Gutierrez</a> in 2005. An armored <a href="/wiki/Isuzu_Trooper" title="Isuzu Trooper">Chevrolet Trooper</a> is also used.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2009)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>. The president travels in one of several armored Nissan Patrol scholastic level 7 for several Ford Explorers, Chevrolet D-Max, Toyota Hilux. In the September 30, 2010 Nissan Patrol withstood high caliber ammunition in the midst of shooting the Police hospital in the city of Quito. The Nissan Patrol fleet was changed for Toyota Land Cruiser 200s.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Egypt">Egypt</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Egypt">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The presidential state car in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a> used by <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> until <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_revolution" title="2011 Egyptian revolution">February 2011</a> was a black armored 1998 <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz" title="Mercedes-Benz">Mercedes-Benz</a> <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">S-Class</a>. An earlier model of it helped save his life in Ethiopia in 1995. The current vehicle used by <a href="/wiki/Abdel_Fattah_el-Sisi" title="Abdel Fattah el-Sisi">Abdel Fattah el-Sisi</a> is a black armored variant of the 2013 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz" title="Mercedes Benz">Mercedes Benz</a> <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">S-Class</a> with a special black number plate with the presidential crest above an Arabic 1. Ministers and highly placed government officials are sometimes seen driving black <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8s</a>, all with special government number plates. Parliamentary vehicles are often <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_E-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz E-Class">Mercedes-Benz E-Class</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="El_Salvador">El Salvador</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: El Salvador">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_El_Salvador" title="President of El Salvador">President of El Salvador</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mauricio_Funes" title="Mauricio Funes">Mauricio Funes</a>, uses an armored <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W220" title="Mercedes-Benz W220">Mercedes-Benz W220</a> as its official state car. He also drives or is driven in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lexus_LX_570" title="Lexus LX 570">Lexus LX 570</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Hummer_H3" title="Hummer H3">Hummer H3</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Jeep_Grand_Cherokee" title="Jeep Grand Cherokee">Jeep Grand Cherokee</a> SRT-8, a <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Suburban" title="Chevrolet Suburban">Chevrolet Suburban</a> and a 200 Series Toyota Land Cruiser. The President is generally escorted by six <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Land_Cruiser_Prado" title="Toyota Land Cruiser Prado">Toyota Land Cruiser Prados</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Estonia">Estonia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Estonia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Vehicle_of_the_Estonian_president.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1724" data-file-width="2832" height="134" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Vehicle_of_the_Estonian_president.JPG/220px-Vehicle_of_the_Estonian_president.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Vehicle_of_the_Estonian_president.JPG/330px-Vehicle_of_the_Estonian_president.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Vehicle_of_the_Estonian_president.JPG/440px-Vehicle_of_the_Estonian_president.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Vehicle_of_the_Estonian_president.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Estonian Presidential car used until 2011. It was replaced with a newer version of the Audi A8L</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>During the first republic (1918–1940), the first President, Konstantin Päts, preferred American cars, such as Studebaker Dictator. After officially becoming a President in 1938, he also bought a Packard Super 8 Touring Sedan, and in next year a Studebaker Commander Cruising Sedan.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Estonia" title="President of Estonia">President of Estonia</a> uses an Audi A8 L 3.0 TDI Quattro Tiptronic with the coat of arms of Estonia as its license plate. The car is escorted by an <a href="/wiki/Audi_Q7" title="Audi Q7">Audi Q7</a>. The Estonian Prime Minister uses an <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a> registered in 2015.</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Finland">Finland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Finland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tasavallanpresidentinvaihdos2012_01.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="501" data-file-width="1272" height="87" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Tasavallanpresidentinvaihdos2012_01.JPG/220px-Tasavallanpresidentinvaihdos2012_01.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Tasavallanpresidentinvaihdos2012_01.JPG/330px-Tasavallanpresidentinvaihdos2012_01.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Tasavallanpresidentinvaihdos2012_01.JPG/440px-Tasavallanpresidentinvaihdos2012_01.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Tasavallanpresidentinvaihdos2012_01.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Finland motorcade</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Finland" title="President of Finland">President of Finland</a> uses an armoured <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S600L</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_Finland" title="Coat of arms of Finland">coat of arms of Finland</a> in lieu of a license plate.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup> A similar car is used by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Speakers_of_the_Parliament_of_Finland" title="Speakers of the Parliament of Finland">Speaker of the Parliament</a>, whereas the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Finland" title="Prime Minister of Finland">Prime Minister</a>'s official car is a grey armoured <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S450 CDI</a>.</p>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Finnish_Council_of_State" title="Finnish Council of State">Finnish cabinet</a> members carpool consist of 8 BMW 525d A xDrive's.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="France">France</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: France">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:PR-2012-05-15_IMG_1733.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3454" data-file-width="5181" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/PR-2012-05-15_IMG_1733.jpg/220px-PR-2012-05-15_IMG_1733.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/PR-2012-05-15_IMG_1733.jpg/330px-PR-2012-05-15_IMG_1733.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/PR-2012-05-15_IMG_1733.jpg/440px-PR-2012-05-15_IMG_1733.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:PR-2012-05-15_IMG_1733.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
President of France <a href="/wiki/Citro%C3%ABn_C6" title="Citroën C6">Citroën C6</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President of France</a> can choose between several armoured versions of high-end French cars including the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Citroen_DS5" title="Citroen DS5">Citroen DS5</a> <a href="/wiki/PSA_HYbrid4" title="PSA HYbrid4">Hybrid4</a>, <a href="/wiki/Citro%C3%ABn_C6" title="Citroën C6">Citroën C6</a>, <a href="/wiki/Renault_Vel_Satis" title="Renault Vel Satis">Renault Vel Satis</a> and <a href="/wiki/Peugeot_607" title="Peugeot 607">Peugeot 607</a>. These are traditionally provided by the manufacturers and different Presidents will have their own preference. <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a> preferred Citroën while <a href="/wiki/Jacques_Chirac" title="Jacques Chirac">Jacques Chirac</a> was a Renault fan, occasionally using his own Renault 5 model and the presidential <a href="/wiki/Citro%C3%ABn_XM" title="Citroën XM">Renault Safrane</a>. President <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Hollande" title="François Hollande">François Hollande</a> is usually chauffeured in an armoured Citroën C6, although he has been known to make private trips by moped.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup></p>
<p>For his <a href="/wiki/Oath_of_office" title="Oath of office">inauguration</a> parade in 2007, Sarkozy used the one-off <a href="/wiki/Peugeot_607" title="Peugeot 607">Peugeot 607</a> Paladine model, a stretched limousine with landaulette body, originally built as a concept car in 2000. The model was brought out of storage for the occasion and updated with a new grille and lights to bring it in line with the 2004 re-style of the mainstream model. It has since been returned to Peugeot and, as it effectively remains a concept car in its fit and finish, will not become part of the <a href="/wiki/%C3%89lys%C3%A9e_Palace" title="Élysée Palace">Élysée</a> fleet. President Hollande used a one-off convertible version of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Citroen_DS5" title="Citroen DS5">Citroen DS5</a> <a href="/wiki/PSA_HYbrid4" title="PSA HYbrid4">Hybrid4</a> for his inauguration parade on May 15, 2012. The car, owned by Citroën, has since been displayed at various events throughout the world.</p>
<p>The most famous association between a President of France and a single model was that of <a href="/wiki/Charles_de_Gaulle" title="Charles de Gaulle">Charles de Gaulle</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Citro%C3%ABn_DS" title="Citroën DS">Citroën DS</a>, as portrayed in the film, <a href="/wiki/The_Day_of_the_Jackal_(film)" title="The Day of the Jackal (film)">Day of the Jackal</a>. The President was saved in two assassination attempts by French <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Algerian_War_of_Independence" title="Algerian War of Independence">Algeria supporters</a> by the car's unique ability to drive on three wheels and to keep running when more than one tyre is punctured.</p>
<p>For ceremonial occasions, the President also has access to two special open top <a href="/wiki/Citro%C3%ABn_SM" title="Citroën SM">Citroën SM</a> Présidentielle models,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup> created for President <a href="/wiki/Georges_Pompidou" title="Georges Pompidou">Georges Pompidou</a> by the coachbuilder <a href="/wiki/Henri_Chapron" title="Henri Chapron">Henri Chapron</a>. Based on the SM Opera, itself a special edition four-door coupé, these cars are still used for state occasions and military parades, when the open-top layout enables the President to stand in the back seat and survey the crowd. Built for an official visit by Queen Elizabeth II in 1972, the cars have a standard mechanical layout with the addition of a special gear for low-speed cruising. One of these cars was also used by President <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Mitterrand" title="François Mitterrand">François Mitterrand</a> for the official opening of the <a href="/wiki/Channel_Tunnel" title="Channel Tunnel">Channel Tunnel</a> in 1994, when it accompanied the Rolls-Royce Phantom VI of Elizabeth II. Number plates on these cars are standard French ones, although specially created for the model (<i>2 PR 75</i> and <i>3 PR 75</i>, '75' denoting the Paris region). Both are still maintained in working order, but are now rarely seen in use.</p>
<p>An international museum of official state cars also exists in France.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Germany">Germany</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Germany">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sonderschutzfahrzeug_des_Bundespr%C3%A4sidenten-02-2.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="2756" height="123" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Sonderschutzfahrzeug_des_Bundespr%C3%A4sidenten-02-2.jpg/220px-Sonderschutzfahrzeug_des_Bundespr%C3%A4sidenten-02-2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Sonderschutzfahrzeug_des_Bundespr%C3%A4sidenten-02-2.jpg/330px-Sonderschutzfahrzeug_des_Bundespr%C3%A4sidenten-02-2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Sonderschutzfahrzeug_des_Bundespr%C3%A4sidenten-02-2.jpg/440px-Sonderschutzfahrzeug_des_Bundespr%C3%A4sidenten-02-2.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sonderschutzfahrzeug_des_Bundespr%C3%A4sidenten-02-2.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The armored <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W221" title="Mercedes-Benz W221">Mercedes-Benz W221</a> used by the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Germany" title="President of Germany">President of Germany</a>, with license plates 0–1</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:AudiA8_Kanzlerwagen.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/AudiA8_Kanzlerwagen.jpg/220px-AudiA8_Kanzlerwagen.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/AudiA8_Kanzlerwagen.jpg/330px-AudiA8_Kanzlerwagen.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/AudiA8_Kanzlerwagen.jpg/440px-AudiA8_Kanzlerwagen.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:AudiA8_Kanzlerwagen.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a> sometimes used by the <a href="/wiki/Chancellor_of_Germany" title="Chancellor of Germany">Chancellor of Germany</a> <a href="/wiki/Angela_Merkel" title="Angela Merkel">Angela Merkel</a>, with license plates 0–2</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Over the years, German presidents, <a href="/wiki/Chancellor_of_Germany" title="Chancellor of Germany">chancellors</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Germany" title="Government of Germany">senior politicians</a> have often used <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a> vehicles and their predecessor models. The most famous variants were the Mercedes 300 series "Adenauer" and the stretched "Pullman" variants. Currently the State Car of the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Germany" title="President of Germany">President of Germany</a> is an armored Mercedes-Benz S600 with license plate <i>0–1</i>, but the president has also used an <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a>. The President is (besides the Minister of Defense) the only German official whose official car regular shows a flag (a version of the President's standard) placed on the front of the hood.</p>
<p>All officials under close personal protection from the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Criminal_Police_Office_(Germany)" title="Federal Criminal Police Office (Germany)">Bundeskriminalamt</a> (BKA), one of Germany's federal police forces; are transported by the BKA pool of armoured cars and BKA driving staff. The car pool includes armored limousines from all German car manufacturers, usually high-end models such as the <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a>, <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Phaeton" title="Volkswagen Phaeton">Volkswagen Phaeton</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a>.</p>
<p>Some German politicians choose to express their regional origins through the make of car they use. In particular officials from Bavaria customarily prefer cars from Munich-based BMW over the more common Mercedes brand. Some high-ranking politicians from <a href="/wiki/Alliance_%2790/The_Greens" title="Alliance '90/The Greens">Alliance '90/The Greens</a> (Germany's green party) have chosen Audi, VW or BMW cars to avoid the posh and elitist image of Mercedes models<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2008)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>. While in office, former Chancellor <a href="/wiki/Gerhard_Schr%C3%B6der" title="Gerhard Schröder">Gerhard Schröder</a> initially used an Audi for his official car, a brand he is known to prefer as his personal car as well. Later during his administrative term, Volkswagen presented him with a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/VW_Phaeton" title="VW Phaeton">VW Phaeton</a> which found its way into the car pool. His successor in office, current Chancellor <a href="/wiki/Angela_Merkel" title="Angela Merkel">Angela Merkel</a> is known to alternate between brands as to project neutrality and support for the German car industry in general.</p>
<p>One of the earliest links between a leader and a particular marque was the association of <a href="/wiki/Paul_von_Hindenburg" title="Paul von Hindenburg">Paul von Hindenburg</a> and <a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> with Mercedes-Benz. Especially Hitler was known for his love of luxury cars and ordered a succession of custom vehicles from Mercedes, culminating in the <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_770" title="Mercedes-Benz 770">770K</a> model of 1941, which was rumoured to weigh up to five tonnes.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup> These cars and their predecessors became synonymous with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nazi" title="Nazi">Nazi</a> parades and Hitler's visits to conquered cities such as <a href="/wiki/Vienna" title="Vienna">Vienna</a> and Paris.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Greece">Greece</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Greece">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Greece" title="Prime Minister of Greece">Prime Minister of Greece</a> used to use a heavy armoured, custom-built <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class_(W221)" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class (W221)">W221</a> <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S600</a> escorted by custom built Mercedes-Benz G-Class vehicles. <a href="/wiki/George_Papandreou" title="George Papandreou">George Papandreou</a> displaced it with a standard <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Prius" title="Toyota Prius">Toyota Prius</a>. On official events the car of the state president was used.</p>
<p>Past PMs have also used a <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Silver_Shadow" title="Rolls-Royce Silver Shadow">Rolls-Royce Silver Shadow</a> Long-Wheelbase Limousine. The president, also, uses a W221 Mercedes-Benz S600, wearing the Greek coat of arms. The monarchs in 1930s used a <a href="/wiki/Maybach_Zeppelin" title="Maybach Zeppelin">Maybach Zeppelin</a>. The official state car of King of Greece in 60s was a 1959 Rolls-Royce Silver Wraith (LHLW44 chassis).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Grenada">Grenada</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Grenada">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Governors-General_of_Grenada" title="List of Governors-General of Grenada">Governor General of Grenada</a> is driven in a white <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_7-Series" title="BMW 7-Series">BMW 750Li</a> with a crown license plate symbolizing the Queen while the Prime Minister drives in a black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_7-Series" title="BMW 7-Series">BMW 750Li</a> bearing a <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Grenada" title="Flag of Grenada">Grenadian flag</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms" title="Coat of arms">coat of arms</a> license plate, escorted by <a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Grenada" title="Law enforcement in Grenada">police</a> motorcycle outriders and two black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Toyota_Landcruiser" title="Toyota Landcruiser">Prado SUVs</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Hungary">Hungary</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Hungary">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Hungarian public key dignitaries and security personnel use armored Audi A8 Ls. Also used in official convoys are the Audi A7, Audi Q7, and Audi A6. The Prime Minister, however, prefers to ride in a Volkswagen Multivan. Members of the Government use the Škoda Superb, while lower-ranking officials use Škoda Octavias.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Hong_Kong">Hong Kong</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Hong Kong">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:LEXUS_LS_600hL_HKSAR_CE_vehicle.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="476" data-file-width="700" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/LEXUS_LS_600hL_HKSAR_CE_vehicle.jpg/220px-LEXUS_LS_600hL_HKSAR_CE_vehicle.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/LEXUS_LS_600hL_HKSAR_CE_vehicle.jpg/330px-LEXUS_LS_600hL_HKSAR_CE_vehicle.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/LEXUS_LS_600hL_HKSAR_CE_vehicle.jpg/440px-LEXUS_LS_600hL_HKSAR_CE_vehicle.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:LEXUS_LS_600hL_HKSAR_CE_vehicle.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS_(XF40)#LS_600h" title="Lexus LS (XF40)">Lexus LS 600h L</a> bearing the HKSAR crest in place of a license plate, the official transport of the <a href="/wiki/Chief_Executive_of_Hong_Kong" title="Chief Executive of Hong Kong">Chief Executive of Hong Kong</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
