<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hong_Kong_SAR_Vehicle_for_the_Chief_Executive.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2448" data-file-width="3264" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Hong_Kong_SAR_Vehicle_for_the_Chief_Executive.JPG/220px-Hong_Kong_SAR_Vehicle_for_the_Chief_Executive.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Hong_Kong_SAR_Vehicle_for_the_Chief_Executive.JPG/330px-Hong_Kong_SAR_Vehicle_for_the_Chief_Executive.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Hong_Kong_SAR_Vehicle_for_the_Chief_Executive.JPG/440px-Hong_Kong_SAR_Vehicle_for_the_Chief_Executive.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hong_Kong_SAR_Vehicle_for_the_Chief_Executive.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_S_Class" title="Mercedes Benz S Class">Mercedes-Benz S500L</a> bearing the HKSAR crest in place of a <a href="/wiki/Vehicle_registration_plates_of_Hong_Kong" title="Vehicle registration plates of Hong Kong">license plate</a>, now used as a spare vehicle for the <a href="/wiki/Chief_Executive_of_Hong_Kong" title="Chief Executive of Hong Kong">Chief Executive of Hong Kong</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>As a special administrative region, official vehicle of the <a href="/wiki/Chief_Executive_of_Hong_Kong" title="Chief Executive of Hong Kong">Chief Executive of Hong Kong</a> bear no license plate but the <a href="/wiki/Emblem_of_Hong_Kong" title="Emblem of Hong Kong">Emblem of Hong Kong</a>. This follows the practice of the British Governor, as the representative of the British Crown, the laws of Hong Kong did not apply to him, including the need for a number plate on his car. Hence the official limousine simply had a Crown emblem front and rear in place of number plates. The current Chief Executive <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CY_Leung" title="CY Leung">CY Leung</a> is usually driven in a Lexus <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS_(XF40)#LS_600h" title="Lexus LS (XF40)">LS 600h L</a> <a href="/wiki/Hybrid_vehicle" title="Hybrid vehicle">hybrid vehicle</a>. Occasionally, the Chief Executive is also seen using a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_S_Class" title="Mercedes Benz S Class">1997 Mercedes-Benz S500L</a>.</p>
<p>Senior government officials, including the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chief_Secretary_of_Hong_Kong" title="Chief Secretary of Hong Kong">Chief Secretary</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chief_Justice_of_the_Court_of_Final_Appeal" title="Chief Justice of the Court of Final Appeal">Chief Justice</a> and Commissioner of Police, are each assigned a <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Phaeton" title="Volkswagen Phaeton">Volkswagen Phaeton</a>. The <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Legislative_Council_of_Hong_Kong" title="President of the Legislative Council of Hong Kong">President of the Legislative Council</a> is driven in a Lexus GS450h, with the number plate "LC1".</p>
<p>Prior to 1997, the <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Hong_Kong" title="Governor of Hong Kong">Governor of Hong Kong</a> used a Rolls-Royce Phantom V for ceremonial occasions and a <a href="/wiki/Daimler_DS420" title="Daimler DS420">Daimler DS420</a> limousine for everyday use. Both were removed from Hong Kong by the Royal Navy immediately following the <a href="/wiki/Transfer_of_sovereignty_over_Hong_Kong" title="Transfer of sovereignty over Hong Kong">handover to China</a> on 1 July 1997. The Phantom V displayed <a href="/wiki/St_Edward%27s_Crown" title="St Edward's Crown">St Edward's Crown</a> instead of a front license plate.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Iceland">Iceland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Iceland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Iceland" title="President of Iceland">President of Iceland</a>, Ólafur Ragnar Grímsson, is driven by a chauffeur in a <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS" title="Lexus LS">Lexus LS</a>600hL with the license plate of "1."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup> For special occasions the president also uses a <a href="/wiki/Packard#1942.E2.80.931945" title="Packard">1942 Packard</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="India">India</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: India">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="President">President</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: President">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:PresidentIndia3.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="998" data-file-width="1871" height="117" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/PresidentIndia3.jpg/220px-PresidentIndia3.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/PresidentIndia3.jpg/330px-PresidentIndia3.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/PresidentIndia3.jpg/440px-PresidentIndia3.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:PresidentIndia3.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
President of India's motorcade, with the official state car.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_India" title="President of India">President of India</a>, travels in a black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S_Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S Class">Mercedes-Benz S Class</a> (S600) Pullman Guard. It is a custom-built, heavily armoured stretch limousine which meets the requirements of the highest protection class <a href="/wiki/EN_1063" title="EN 1063">BR7-level</a>. The President's motorcade also always consists of the former presidential car, a black <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz" title="Mercedes-Benz">Mercedes-Benz</a> armoured limousine, which is used as a spare vehicle. Along with it, is a white <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz" title="Mercedes-Benz">Mercedes-Benz</a> ambulance, black <a href="/wiki/Tata_Safari" title="Tata Safari">Tata Safari</a> SUVs and a few black sedans. The presidential car displays the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Emblem_of_India" title="Emblem of India">National Emblem of India</a> instead of the number plates.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup> They are protected and followed by the <a href="/wiki/President%27s_Bodyguard" title="President's Bodyguard">President's Bodyguard</a>.</p>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_India" title="Vice President of India">Vice President of India</a> uses a white <a href="/wiki/EN_1063" title="EN 1063">BR7-level</a> armoured 2009 <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series_(F01)#760Li_High_Security_and_750Li_High_Security_.28F03.29" title="BMW 7 Series (F01)">BMW 7 Series High Security</a> saloon. It also has the National Emblem (Coat of Arms) instead of the number plates.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Prime_Minister_2">Prime Minister</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Prime Minister">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_India" title="Prime Minister of India">Prime Minister of India</a>, the head of the government, uses two black, <a href="/wiki/EN_1063" title="EN 1063">BR7-level</a> highly modified armoured <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series_(F01)" title="BMW 7 Series (F01)">BMW 7 Series (F01)</a> with one used as a decoy. These are escorted by the <a href="/wiki/Special_Protection_Group" title="Special Protection Group">SPG</a> in six armoured black <a href="/wiki/BMW_X5_(E70)#E70_Second_Generation.282006-2013.29" title="BMW X5 (E70)">BMW X5s</a>, and a few <a href="/wiki/Tata_Safari" title="Tata Safari">Tata Safaris</a> with one equipped with a <a href="/wiki/Counter-IED_equipment" title="Counter-IED equipment">jammer</a> which are a permanent part of the Prime Minister's convoy. When visiting a foreign country, Indian leaders generally use vehicles supplied by the host country.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Indonesia">Indonesia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Indonesia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Indonesia" title="President of Indonesia">President of Indonesia</a> is driven in one of two armored black <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class_(W221)" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class (W221)">Mercedes-Benz S600 Guard</a> bearing the "RI 1" or "INDONESIA 1" license plate and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Indonesian_flag" title="Indonesian flag">Indonesian flag</a>.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_Indonesia" title="Vice President of Indonesia">Vice President of Indonesia</a> is driven in a similar car, bearing the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Indonesian_flag" title="Indonesian flag">Indonesian flag</a> and a "RI 2" or "INDONESIA 2" license plate.</p>
<p>The President and Vice President of Indonesia are escorted by the <a href="/wiki/Paspampres" title="Paspampres">Presidential Security Forces</a> in a number of cars depending on the security detail, where the fleet consists of <a href="/wiki/BMW_X5_(E70)" title="BMW X5 (E70)">BMW X5</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_G-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz G-Class">Mercedes-Benz G-Class</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nissan_Patrol" title="Nissan Patrol">Nissan Patrol</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nissan_X-Trail" title="Nissan X-Trail">Nissan X-Trail</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Fortuner" title="Toyota Fortuner">Toyota Fortuner</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Land_Cruiser" title="Toyota Land Cruiser">Toyota Land Cruiser</a> models as well as a <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Transporter_(T5)" title="Volkswagen Transporter (T5)">Volkswagen Caravelle</a> carrying a communications jammer device.</p>
<p>In addition to the escort cars, the Security Forces sometimes also consist of two <a href="/wiki/Yamaha_FZ1" title="Yamaha FZ1">Yamaha FZ1</a> motorcycles</p>
<p>The Presidential Fleet also contains other vehicles such as <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series_(F01)" title="BMW 7 Series (F01)">BMW 760Li Security</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_X5_(E70)" title="BMW X5 (E70)">BMW X5 Security</a>, the previously used <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W140" title="Mercedes-Benz W140">Mercedes-Benz S600 Guard</a> as well as a newer <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class_(W222)" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class (W222)">Mercedes-Benz S600 Guard</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Land_Cruiser" title="Toyota Land Cruiser">Toyota Land Cruiser</a> models, all armored and in black.</p>
<p>For trips outside <a href="/wiki/Jakarta" title="Jakarta">Jakarta</a> the SUV models are preferred to the usual Mercedes limousine. During military exercises, the President of Indonesia is driven in armored personnel carriers bearing the 'INDONESIA 1" license plate, usually in the <a href="/wiki/Anoa_(armoured_personnel_carrier)" title="Anoa (armoured personnel carrier)">Anoa</a>. An older <a href="/wiki/BMW_X5_(E53)" title="BMW X5 (E53)">BMW X5</a> was notably used by former president <a href="/wiki/Susilo_Bambang_Yudhoyono" title="Susilo Bambang Yudhoyono">Susilo Bambang Yudhoyono</a> during the <a href="/wiki/2007_Jakarta_flood" title="2007 Jakarta flood">2007 Jakarta flood</a>.</p>
<p>Cabinet ministers of Indonesia are driven in black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Toyota_Crown_Hybrid" title="Toyota Crown Hybrid">Toyota Crown</a> models, escorted by black <a href="/wiki/Nissan_X-Trail" title="Nissan X-Trail">Nissan X-Trail</a> or <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Fortuner" title="Toyota Fortuner">Toyota Fortuner</a> vehicles.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Indonesian_National_Police" title="Indonesian National Police">Indonesian National Police</a> is present in all motorcades.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Iran">Iran</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Iran">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Hassan_Rouhani" title="Hassan Rouhani">current president of Iran</a> has used different vehicles over the years ranging from <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Cressida" title="Toyota Cressida">Toyota Cressida</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a> and recently a <a href="/wiki/Peugeot_607" title="Peugeot 607">Peugeot 607</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad" title="Mahmoud Ahmadinejad">former president of Iran</a>, used a 1977 <a href="/wiki/Peugeot_504" title="Peugeot 504">Peugeot 504</a>. Cars for diplomatic and official purposes range from various types of Mercedes-Benz, BMW and Peugeot, through to domestically-made <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Samand" title="Samand">Samand</a> model Sarir.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Iraq">Iraq</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Iraq">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Iraqi President uses a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E67" title="BMW E67">BMW E67 760 Li</a> escorted by <a href="/wiki/Nissan_Patrol" title="Nissan Patrol">Nissan Patrol</a> models. The Prime Minister uses an armoured <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chevy_Tahoe" title="Chevy Tahoe">Chevy Tahoe</a> along with a Toyota Land Cruiser and <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Suburban" title="Chevrolet Suburban">Chevrolet Suburban</a>.</p>
<p>While in power, <a href="/wiki/Saddam_Hussein" title="Saddam Hussein">Saddam Hussein</a> normally traveled in a <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W126" title="Mercedes-Benz W126">Mercedes-Benz W126</a>, and also bought a large fleet of luxury cars for himself and his family. Some were classic American cars, many from the era of <a href="/wiki/Al_Capone" title="Al Capone">Al Capone</a> of whom Saddam Hussein was an admirer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ireland">Ireland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Ireland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The daily transport for the <a href="/wiki/Taoiseach" title="Taoiseach">Taoiseach</a> (Prime Minister) of Ireland is a black 2014 <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a>, a 3.0 litre diesel, or a dark coloured 2013 <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a> 3.0 TDI Quattro model with 242 bhp, replacing the previous 2006 <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a>. The Taoiseach is driven by specially trained and armed members of the Garda <a href="/wiki/Special_Detective_Unit" title="Special Detective Unit">Special Detective Unit</a> (SDU). The car the Taoiseach travels in is always accompanied by a follow car, usually an identical Audi A6 or BMW 7 Series, or an unmarked <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a> (2.5 petrol), containing armed close protection officers from the SDU and staff/minders. The Taoiseach's car is usually escorted by motorcycle outriders from the <a href="/wiki/Garda_Traffic_Corps" title="Garda Traffic Corps">Garda Traffic Corps</a>, and further marked and unmarked patrol cars are added to the escort when the Taoiseach is attending sensitive events or during times of a heightened security risk. The <a href="/wiki/T%C3%A1naiste" title="Tánaiste">Tánaiste</a> (Deputy Prime Minister) usually travels in a similar Audi A6.</p>
<p>The daily transport of the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Ireland" title="President of Ireland">President of Ireland</a> is a black 2006 <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a> (3.5 petrol). The President receives the highest protection in the land by law. The President's car is driven by a specially trained and armed member of the Garda Special Branch. The motorcade is led by Garda motorbikes to fend off traffic for the oncoming motorcade. A marked patrol car follows and then the President's car proceeds. Two unmarked cars from the Special Detective Unit follow, they are usually <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a>, <a href="/wiki/Volvo_S60" title="Volvo S60">Volvo S60</a> and/or <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a>, containing armed bodyguards and the President's staff. The President's <i><a href="/wiki/Aide-de-camp" title="Aide-de-camp">Aide-de-camp</a></i> always travels with him in the cavalcade. The convoy occasionally contains a vehicle from the <a href="/wiki/Garda_Emergency_Response_Unit" title="Garda Emergency Response Unit">Garda Emergency Response Unit</a> (ERU) for increased security.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Presidential_State_Car_(Ireland)" title="Presidential State Car (Ireland)">Presidential State Car</a> is a <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Silver_Wraith" title="Rolls-Royce Silver Wraith">Rolls-Royce Silver Wraith</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Landaulette" title="Landaulette">landaulette</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vehicle_registration_plates_of_Ireland" title="Vehicle registration plates of Ireland">license plate</a> ZJ 5000, nicknamed "DeV's car" because of its association with former President <a href="/wiki/%C3%89amon_de_Valera" title="Éamon de Valera">Éamon de Valera</a>. It is only used occasionally by the President for ceremonial occasions.</p>
<p>Uniquely in Ireland, politicians (Taoiseach, Tánaiste, Ministers) usually sit in the front of the car while the President sits in the back.</p>
<p>Full-time armed protection and transport is also afforded to; the <a href="/wiki/T%C3%A1naiste" title="Tánaiste">Tánaiste</a>, <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Justice_and_Equality" title="Minister for Justice and Equality">Minister for Justice and Equality</a>, <a href="/wiki/Attorney_General_of_Ireland" title="Attorney General of Ireland">Attorney General</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chief_Justice_of_Ireland" title="Chief Justice of Ireland">Chief Justice</a>, <a href="/wiki/Director_of_Public_Prosecutions" title="Director of Public Prosecutions">Director of Public Prosecutions</a> and <a href="/wiki/Police_commissioner" title="Police commissioner">Garda Commissioner</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup> All government ministers and former Presidents and Taoisigh are provided with armed protection and transport when their security is deemed under threat, otherwise it is reserved for official state occasions.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ambassadors" title="Ambassadors">Ambassadors</a> and high-ranking foreign diplomats in Ireland are given protection by the SDU when their safety or security is "at risk", such as the Ambassadors of the United Kingdom, United States and <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> in Dublin.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup> This fleet includes <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_E-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz E-Class">Mercedes-Benz E-Class</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a>, <a href="/wiki/Volvo_S60" title="Volvo S60">Volvo S60</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lexus_GS" title="Lexus GS">Lexus GS</a>. A fleet of armoured vehicles are deployed for visiting dignitaries, such as heads of state.</p>
<p>When the President or Taoiseach visits <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>, they are driven in armoured vehicles and security in their motorcade increases. The Garda SDU and ERU liaise with the <a href="/wiki/Police_Service_of_Northern_Ireland" title="Police Service of Northern Ireland">Police Service of Northern Ireland</a> (PSNI) Close Protection Unit (CPU) during visits to Northern Ireland.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Israel">Israel</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Israel">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Israeli_Government_Official_Car_-_Volvo_S80_Stretch_Limousine_-_Front.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2529" data-file-width="2367" height="235" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Israeli_Government_Official_Car_-_Volvo_S80_Stretch_Limousine_-_Front.jpg/220px-Israeli_Government_Official_Car_-_Volvo_S80_Stretch_Limousine_-_Front.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Israeli_Government_Official_Car_-_Volvo_S80_Stretch_Limousine_-_Front.jpg/330px-Israeli_Government_Official_Car_-_Volvo_S80_Stretch_Limousine_-_Front.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Israeli_Government_Official_Car_-_Volvo_S80_Stretch_Limousine_-_Front.jpg/440px-Israeli_Government_Official_Car_-_Volvo_S80_Stretch_Limousine_-_Front.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>

</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel" title="Prime Minister of Israel">Prime Minister of Israel</a> uses a fleet of Toyota Land Cruisers, Lexus IS 250, <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Volvo_S80" title="Volvo S80">Volvo S80</a>. The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Israel" title="President of Israel">President of Israel</a> uses a <a href="/wiki/Volvo_Cars" title="Volvo Cars">Volvo</a> stretch limousine and <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a>.</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Italy">Italy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Italy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tmulti tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:224px;max-width:224px">
<div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:222px;max-width:222px">
<div class="thumbimage"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:2june_2007_615.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="1944" data-file-width="2592" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/2june_2007_615.jpg/220px-2june_2007_615.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/2june_2007_615.jpg/330px-2june_2007_615.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/2june_2007_615.jpg/440px-2june_2007_615.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a></div>
<div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left"><a href="/wiki/Lancia_Thesis" title="Lancia Thesis">Lancia Thesis</a>, official state car of Italy.</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In 1960 the then <a href="/wiki/President_of_Italy" title="President of Italy">President of Italy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Giovanni_Gronchi" title="Giovanni Gronchi">Giovanni Gronchi</a>, personally ordered custom-built <a href="/wiki/Lancia_Flaminia" title="Lancia Flaminia">Lancia Flaminia</a> limousines for a state visit by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Elizabeth II of the United Kingdom">Queen Elizabeth II</a>. Four <a href="/wiki/Lancia_Flaminia#355_Presidenziale.2FQuirinale" title="Lancia Flaminia">Lancia Flaminia 355 Presidenziale</a> were delivered, coachbuilt by <a href="/wiki/Pininfarina" title="Pininfarina">Pininfarina</a> with <a href="/wiki/Landaulet" title="Landaulet">landaulet</a> body on an extended wheelbase. All of the original four cars survive today, with two being leased to different automobile museums and two still in service for most solemn state occasions, like the <a href="/wiki/Festa_della_Repubblica#The_parade" title="Festa della Repubblica">Republic Day parade</a> or presidential inaugurations.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup> <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Sandro_Pertini" title="Sandro Pertini">Sandro Pertini</a> drove a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maserati_Quattroporte_III" title="Maserati Quattroporte III">Maserati Quattroporte III</a> during his tenure.</p>
<p>The current presidential cars are two identical armoured <a href="/wiki/Lancia_Thesis" title="Lancia Thesis">Lancia Thesis</a>, with a third unarmoured one kept as backup. In 2012 a fourth armoured Thesis was delivered by Lancia. A <a href="/wiki/Lancia_Thesis#Lancia_Thesis_Stola_S85" title="Lancia Thesis">Lancia Thesis Stola S85</a> limousine and three <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maserati_Quattroporte_V" title="Maserati Quattroporte V">Maserati Quattroporte</a> are at the disposal of visiting foreign presidents.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup></p>
<p>There is also a curious three-wheeled <a href="/wiki/Piaggio_Ape" title="Piaggio Ape">Piaggio Ape Calessino</a>, in service at the presidential summer residence <a href="/wiki/Villa_Rosebery" title="Villa Rosebery">Villa Rosebery</a> and therefore rarely seen. It was donated in 2008 by <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Roberto_Colaninno&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Roberto Colaninno (page does not exist)">Roberto Colaninno</a>, head of <a href="/wiki/Piaggio" title="Piaggio">Piaggio</a> industries, on the 60th anniversary of both the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian_Constitution" title="Italian Constitution">Italian Constitution</a> and Calessino. Its blue livery is decorated with the emblem of the Presidency of the Italian Republic, while the interior is trimmed in wood and white leather.</p>
<p>The government fleet includes a varied array of vehicles, notably <a href="/wiki/Alfa_Romeo_159" title="Alfa Romeo 159">Alfa Romeo 159</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alfa_Romeo_166" title="Alfa Romeo 166">166</a>, <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6#C6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a> and <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8#D3" title="Audi A8">A8</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Continental_Flying_Spur" title="Bentley Continental Flying Spur">Bentley Continental Flying Spur</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series_(E60)" title="BMW 5 Series (E60)">BMW 5 Series</a> and <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series_(E65)" title="BMW 7 Series (E65)">7 Series</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lancia_Thesis" title="Lancia Thesis">Lancia Thesis</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lancia_Thema" title="Lancia Thema">Lancia Thema</a>, <a href="/wiki/Maserati_Quattroporte" title="Maserati Quattroporte">Maserati Quattroporte</a> V and VI, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W212" title="Mercedes-Benz W212">Mercedes-Benz W212</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W221" title="Mercedes-Benz W221">W221</a> models.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Jamaica">Jamaica</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Jamaica">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Governor-General_of_Jamaica" title="Governor-General of Jamaica">Governor-General of Jamaica</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Jamaica" title="Prime Minister of Jamaica">Prime Minister of Jamaica</a> are both driven in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W221" title="Mercedes-Benz W221">Mercedes-Benz W221</a> bearing the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jamaican_flag" title="Jamaican flag">Jamaican flag</a> and the standard of that office. The Governor-General's car carries license plate is "GG1"; whilst the Prime Minister's car carries government plates (yellow plate with black letters). Ministers generally use a gray <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Toyota_Prado" title="Toyota Prado">Toyota Prado</a> or <a href="/wiki/Mitsubishi_Pajero" title="Mitsubishi Pajero">Mitsubishi Pajero</a>, bearing either government plates or civilian plates with tags.</p>
<p>Previous vehicles used by holders of these offices include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Dark Blue <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a>.</li>
<li>Black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_S600" title="Mercedes Benz S600">Mercedes Benz S600</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Japan">Japan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Japan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Imperial_Processional_Car.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1080" data-file-width="1920" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Imperial_Processional_Car.jpg/220px-Imperial_Processional_Car.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Imperial_Processional_Car.jpg/330px-Imperial_Processional_Car.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Imperial_Processional_Car.jpg/440px-Imperial_Processional_Car.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Imperial_Processional_Car.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Toyota Century Royal</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The official state car currently used by the <a href="/wiki/Emperor_of_Japan" title="Emperor of Japan">Emperor of Japan</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Imperial_House_of_Japan" title="Imperial House of Japan">Empress of Japan</a> is a specially prepared <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Toyota_Century_Royal" title="Toyota Century Royal">Toyota Century Royal</a>, a one-off $500,000 custom car. Custom built by <a href="/wiki/Toyota" title="Toyota">Toyota</a>, it is 20 feet (6.1 m) long and 6.5 feet (2.0 m) wide, with extra amenities such as bulletproofing and a granite entryway.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup> The Emperor was previously transported in multiple vehicles including a <a href="/wiki/Nissan_Prince_Royal" title="Nissan Prince Royal">Nissan Prince Royal</a> (1967–2008), <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_Series_70" title="Cadillac Series 70">Cadillac Series 75</a> (1951–1970), <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_770" title="Mercedes-Benz 770">Mercedes-Benz 770 W07 Series</a> (1932–1968), <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Silver_Ghost" title="Rolls-Royce Silver Ghost">Rolls-Royce Silver Ghost</a> (1921–1936) and a <a href="/wiki/Daimler_Company#Owned_by_BSA_.281910-1960.29" title="Daimler Company">Daimler</a> (1913–1927). From 1935 to 1963, the royal household also possessed a fleet of five 1935 <a href="/wiki/Packard_Eight" title="Packard Eight">Packard Eights</a>, one of which was Emperor Hirohito's personal car during that period.The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Japan" title="Prime Minister of Japan">Prime Minister of Japan</a> travels in a Lexus <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS_(XF40)#LS_600h" title="Lexus LS (XF40)">LS 600h L</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jp_46-0"><a href="#cite_note-jp-46">[46]</a></sup> the official transport for the head of government, or an unmodified <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Century" title="Toyota Century">Toyota Century</a> escorted by a <a href="/wiki/Security_Police_(Japan)" title="Security Police (Japan)">police</a> motorcade of numerous <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Toyota_Celsior" title="Toyota Celsior">Toyota Celsiors</a></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Kenya">Kenya</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Kenya">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kibaki_Land_Rover.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="333" data-file-width="500" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/2/21/Kibaki_Land_Rover.jpg/220px-Kibaki_Land_Rover.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/2/21/Kibaki_Land_Rover.jpg/330px-Kibaki_Land_Rover.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/2/21/Kibaki_Land_Rover.jpg/440px-Kibaki_Land_Rover.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Kibaki_Land_Rover.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Former President <a href="/wiki/Mwai_Kibaki" title="Mwai Kibaki">Mwai Kibaki</a> in the ceremonial Land Rover 109</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Kenya" title="President of Kenya">President</a> of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republic_of_Kenya" title="Republic of Kenya">Republic of Kenya</a> has several official cars that he uses during his travels. The most common one that he uses is an armoured Mercedes Benz Pullman S600 with the Kenyan coat of arms instead of the licence plate. The other fleet he normally uses from time to time includes an armoured Range Rover Vogue, armoured Toyota Landcruiser and several other Mercedes-Benz's at his disposal. Additionally, he has an open top military Land Cruiser, covered with bullet proof glass on the side, used during state functions with licence plates CIC (Commander In Chief). For a long time an open top military Land Rover 109 was used during state ceremonies but it was retired by the Land Cruiser. His escort includes several Mercedes-Benz E-classes, BMW 5 series, a Range Rover, Toyota Landcruisers and an ambulance. Cabinet ministers are supplied with Volkswagen Passats, Mercedes Benz E &amp; S – classes and Toyota Landcruisers in addition to other vehicles in the ministerial car pool. The Prime Minister in office from 2008–2013 was equipped with similar vehicles to the president; Mercedes-benz limousines, Range Rovers and Landcruisers, however, he had a substantially smaller escort.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Kuwait">Kuwait</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Kuwait">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Emir_of_Kuwait" title="Emir of Kuwait">Emir of Kuwait</a> uses a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_7-series" title="BMW 7-series">BMW 7-series</a> or <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a> on a daily basis. His motorcade consists of three identical cars escorted by <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Suburban" title="Chevrolet Suburban">Chevrolet Suburbans</a> and marked police vehicles. For state occasions he uses a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_(car)" title="Rolls-Royce (car)">Rolls-Royce</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Laos">Laos</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Laos">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The daily transport of the president of Laos is a <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Crown" title="Toyota Crown">Toyota Crown</a>. Prime Minister official cars include <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Vito" title="Mercedes Vito">Mercedes Vito</a> and Toyota Crown, while Politburo members travel in <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a> (C6).</p>
<p>Cabinet ministers and vice minister official cars is <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Camry" title="Toyota Camry">Toyota Camry</a> (XV40) and <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Corolla" title="Toyota Corolla">Toyota Corolla</a> respectively. Visiting heads of state or government are chauffeured in a Toyota Crown.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Latvia">Latvia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Latvia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The President of Latvia travels in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S500" title="Mercedes-Benz S500">Mercedes-Benz S500</a>, with the <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_Latvia" title="Coat of arms of Latvia">coat of arms of Latvia</a> as the number plate and front mounted Latvian flag.</p>
<p>Most Latvian Parliament members use <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Volvo_900_series" title="Volvo 900 series">Volvo 900 series</a>, <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_E-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz E-Class">Mercedes-Benz E-Class</a> cars, but also <a href="/wiki/Volvo_S80" title="Volvo S80">Volvo S80</a>, <a href="/wiki/Volvo_S70" title="Volvo S70">Volvo S70</a> and other luxury sedans are in use.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Lebanon">Lebanon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Lebanon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The president's car is a W221 Mercedes-Benz S600Guard armoured limousine and it is escorted by the Republican Guard's SUVs and other security vehicles including the preceding official state car, an armoured W140 S600 now possibly used as a back up limo.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47"><a href="#cite_note-47">[47]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49"><a href="#cite_note-49">[49]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Liberia">Liberia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Liberia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The current <a href="/wiki/President_of_Liberia" title="President of Liberia">President of Liberia</a> is driven in a black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W220" title="Mercedes-Benz W220">Mercedes-Benz W220</a> S-class. The presidential car is often escorted by several Nissan SUVs carrying security personnel. Previous presidents, such as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charles_Taylor_(Liberia)" title="Charles Taylor (Liberia)">Charles Taylor</a> and <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Doe" title="Samuel Doe">Samuel Doe</a>, were also driven in Mercedes-Benz. Some claim that Doe had purchased over 60 luxury Mercedes, which cost over US$60,000 each<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2008)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Lithuania">Lithuania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Lithuania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The first official <a href="/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a> state car was bought in 1919 from war-losing Germany. It was a Benz 25/55PS with four cylinder, 6.3 liter engine. The car had a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vytis" title="Vytis">Vytis</a> symbol on the left back door and Lithuania flags in the front. The car was used by <a href="/wiki/Antanas_Smetona" title="Antanas Smetona">Antanas Smetona</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aleksandras_Stulginskis" title="Aleksandras Stulginskis">Aleksandras Stulginskis</a>. Later Lithuania bought a French-made <a href="/wiki/Delaunay-Belleville" title="Delaunay-Belleville">Delauney-Belleville 12 CV</a> which was used along with Benz 25/55PS by third Lithuania president <a href="/wiki/Kazys_Grinius" title="Kazys Grinius">Kazys Grinius</a>. After that Antanas Smetona became president of Lithuania again and ordered to buy a new car – <a href="/wiki/Fiat_519" title="Fiat 519">Fiat 519</a>, however soon it was replaced with armored <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_K-series" title="Lincoln K-series">Lincoln K-series</a> due to his wife wishes. None of these cars remained until nowadays. After the restoration of Lithuania independence, leader of The Supreme Council, <a href="/wiki/Vytautas_Landsbergis" title="Vytautas Landsbergis">Vytautas Landsbergis</a> used Soviet-built <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chaika_(car)" title="Chaika (car)">Čaika M14</a>, after some time it was replaced with armored <a href="/wiki/Opel_Senator" title="Opel Senator">Opel Senator</a>. Later Lithuania bought armored <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W126" title="Mercedes-Benz W126">Mercedes-Benz W126</a>, which was used by Vytautas Landsbergis and <a href="/wiki/Algirdas_Brazauskas" title="Algirdas Brazauskas">Algirdas Brazauskas</a>. The car is now owned by businessman Robertas Dargis. During Algirdas Brazauskas term of office, two brand-new <a href="/wiki/Audi_V8" title="Audi V8">Audi V8 Lang</a> arrived, later they were replaced with newer version <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8 Lang</a>. <a href="/wiki/Valdas_Adamkus" title="Valdas Adamkus">Valdas Adamkus</a> was driven in a long-wheel base <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_7" title="BMW 7">BMW 7</a> for a short amount of time, however later it was replaced with <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class#W220_.281999.29" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class (W220)</a>, which was used until 2013.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup> In 2013, four armoured <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series_(F01)#BMW_7_Series_High_Security_.282012-.29" title="BMW 7 Series (F01)">BMW 7 (F01)</a> was purchased.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Luxembourg">Luxembourg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Luxembourg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grand-duke" title="Grand-duke">grand-duke</a> and family are driven in <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a>. For official occasions like <a href="/wiki/State_visit" title="State visit">state visits</a> and royal weddings there is a <a href="/wiki/Daimler_DS420" title="Daimler DS420">Daimler DS420</a> and also a <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Mulsanne_(2010)" title="Bentley Mulsanne (2010)">Bentley Mulsanne</a>. Most of the royal cars are dark blue.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Macau">Macau</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Macau">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Chief_Executive_of_Macau" title="Chief Executive of Macau">Chief Executive of Macau</a> is driven in a fleet of government vehicles with special plates reserved for government officials. The fleet consists of European cars, namely <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz" title="Mercedes-Benz">Mercedes-Benz</a>, <a href="/wiki/Audi" title="Audi">Audi</a> or <a href="/wiki/Volvo" title="Volvo">Volvo</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Macedonia">Macedonia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Macedonia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Macedonia" title="Prime Minister of Macedonia">Prime Minister of Macedonia</a> is driven in an armored <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class_(W222)" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class (W222)">Mercedes-Benz S-Class (W222)</a> and escorted by four <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Skoda_Superb" title="Skoda Superb">Skoda Superb</a>. The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Macedonia" title="President of Macedonia">President of Macedonia</a> is driven by stretched <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W140" title="Mercedes-Benz W140">Mercedes-Benz W140</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Malaysia">Malaysia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Malaysia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Yang_di-Pertuan_Agong_and_other_Malaysian_Sultans">Yang di-Pertuan Agong and other Malaysian Sultans</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Yang di-Pertuan Agong and other Malaysian Sultans">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Maybach_of_Yang_di-Pertuan_Agong.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1092" data-file-width="1587" height="151" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Maybach_of_Yang_di-Pertuan_Agong.jpg/220px-Maybach_of_Yang_di-Pertuan_Agong.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Maybach_of_Yang_di-Pertuan_Agong.jpg/330px-Maybach_of_Yang_di-Pertuan_Agong.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Maybach_of_Yang_di-Pertuan_Agong.jpg/440px-Maybach_of_Yang_di-Pertuan_Agong.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">

</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">

</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Yang_di-Pertuan_Agong" title="Yang di-Pertuan Agong">Yang di-Pertuan Agong</a> travels in either a stretched red <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Arnage" title="Bentley Arnage">Bentley Arnage</a>, a dark-blue <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Continental_Flying_Spur_(2005)" title="Bentley Continental Flying Spur (2005)">Bentley Continental Flying Spur</a>, or black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maybach_62" title="Maybach 62">Maybach 62</a>.</p>
<p>All the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Malay_Ruler" title="Malay Ruler">Sultans</a> in Malaysia are also transported in official cars bearing their respective royal emblems; common choices include <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_(2003)" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom (2003)">Rolls-Royce Phantom</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS" title="Lexus LS">Lexus LS</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maybach_62" title="Maybach 62">Maybach 62</a>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Prime_Minister_3">Prime Minister</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Prime Minister">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Under the guidelines of Malaysia's automotive policies, cars for use by <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Malaysia" title="Government of Malaysia">federal and state government</a> officials are required to be of national makes<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Local_state_cars_53-0"><a href="#cite_note-Local_state_cars-53">[53]</a></sup> primarily <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Proton_(carmaker)" title="Proton (carmaker)">Proton</a>.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Malaysia" title="Prime Minister of Malaysia">Prime Minister</a> uses a stretched <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Second_generation_Proton_Perdana" title="Second generation Proton Perdana">Proton Perdana</a> which features classified security measures to protect occupants of the vehicle.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Malawi">Malawi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Malawi">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Malawi" title="President of Malawi">President of Malawi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bingu_wa_Mutharika" title="Bingu wa Mutharika">Bingu wa Mutharika</a>, was driven in an armored Black Mercedes Benz S Class, a Toyota Land Cruiser or Range Rover, the security features remain a state secret. The President traveled in a motorcade of four Hummer H3 and eight escort motorcycles, along with police cars.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Malta">Malta</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Malta">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Among the presidential cars are a pair of <a href="/wiki/Vanden_Plas_Princess" title="Vanden Plas Princess">Vanden Plas Princess</a> limousines, one dating from 1960 and the other, a convertible, from 1955. Both remain in use for state visits and similar occasions; they were originally imported and used by the British <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Governor_of_Malta" title="Governor of Malta">Governor of Malta</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Mauritius">Mauritius</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Mauritius">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Prime Minister of The Republic of Mauritius uses an armored <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a> on a daily basis. He is escorted by one <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a> and five police motorcycles. The President of the Republic of Mauritius uses a BMW 750Li. She is escorted by a <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a> and at least two police motorcycles.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Mexico">Mexico</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Mexico">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Mexico" title="President of Mexico">President</a> and <a href="/wiki/First_Lady_of_Mexico" title="First Lady of Mexico">First Lady</a> of <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a> both possess a fleet of 30 armoured <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Suburban" title="Chevrolet Suburban">Chevrolet Suburban</a>, managed by the <a href="/wiki/Estado_Mayor_Presidencial" title="Estado Mayor Presidencial">Estado Mayor Presidencial</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="A reliable and definite source is needed for this statement. (June 2013)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Moldova">Moldova</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Moldova">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Moldova" title="President of Moldova">President</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Moldova" title="Prime Minister of Moldova">Prime Minister</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Moldovan_Parliament" title="President of the Moldovan Parliament">Speaker of the Parliament</a> of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republic_of_Moldova" title="Republic of Moldova">Republic of Moldova</a> have three long-wheelbase <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_S500" title="Mercedes Benz S500">Mercedes Benz S500s</a> at their disposal, all of which were purchased in 2012 and are operated by the State Protection and Guard Service. The vehicles are not armoured.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="The validity and legitimacy of this statement is unknown. (June 2013)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Morocco">Morocco</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Morocco">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/King_of_Morocco" title="King of Morocco">King of Morocco</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muhammad_VI_of_Morocco" title="Muhammad VI of Morocco">Muhammad VI</a> Normally, when inside Morocco he uses his <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_600" title="Mercedes-Benz 600">Mercedes 600 Pullman</a>. The royal fleet also includes <a href="/wiki/Range_Rover" title="Range Rover">Range Rover</a> models (when he goes to mountainous places only), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S500" title="Mercedes-Benz S500">Mercedes-Benz S500</a> and various <a href="/wiki/Lexus" title="Lexus">Lexus</a> models. One <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_5-series" title="BMW 5-series">BMW 5-series</a>, which travels in the King’s motorcade, contains a communications jammer. An ambulance is always present in the royal motorcade, which is usually escorted by police motorcycles.</p>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Morocco" title="Prime Minister of Morocco">Prime Minister of Morocco</a> is driven in a <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a>, like all other ministers. The King also has a personal garage, which consists of a lot of sports cars, including three <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fulgura" title="Fulgura">Laraki Fulgura</a> models, and an <a href="/wiki/Aston_Martin_DB7" title="Aston Martin DB7">Aston Martin DB7</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Monaco">Monaco</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Monaco">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In 2011, <a href="/wiki/Albert_II,_Prince_of_Monaco" title="Albert II, Prince of Monaco">Prince Albert II</a> acquired a one off <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS_(XF40)#LS_600h_L_Landaulet" title="Lexus LS (XF40)">Lexus LS 600h L Landaulet</a> hybrid sedan, making it his official state car.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56"><a href="#cite_note-56">[56]</a></sup> In addition, he owns a variety of eco friendly cars including a <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS_(XF40)" title="Lexus LS (XF40)">Lexus LS 600h</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_Hydrogen_7" title="BMW Hydrogen 7">BMW Hydrogen 7</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Prius" title="Toyota Prius">Toyota Prius</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lexus_RX_400h" title="Lexus RX 400h">Lexus RX 400h</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fisker_Karma" title="Fisker Karma">Fisker Karma</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tesla_Roadster" title="Tesla Roadster">Tesla Roadster</a>, and a limited production <a href="/wiki/Venturi_F%C3%A9tish" title="Venturi Fétish">Venturi Fétish</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57"><a href="#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59"><a href="#cite_note-59">[59]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61"><a href="#cite_note-61">[61]</a></sup> He also owns a collection of vintage cars, which number over 100, and include prestigious models from <a href="/wiki/Maserati" title="Maserati">Maserati</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_Cars" title="Jaguar Cars">Jaguar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz" title="Mercedes-Benz">Mercedes</a>, Rolls-Royce and <a href="/wiki/Bentley" title="Bentley">Bentley</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup></p>
<p>Government and escorting security officials drive a fleet of <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS_(XF40)" title="Lexus LS (XF40)">Lexus LS 600h</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_Motorrad" title="BMW Motorrad">BMW Motorcycles</a>, and <a href="/wiki/KTM" title="KTM">KTM</a> for out riding.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Mongolia">Mongolia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Mongolia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Mongolia" title="President of Mongolia">President of Mongolia</a> uses a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes Benz S-Class">Mercedes Benz S-Class</a> with number plate 0001, the Speaker of the Parliament a S-Class with number plate 0002 and the Prime Minister a S-Class with number plate 0003, all escorted by a traffic police car and either a Land Cruiser Series 100 or 200, all protected by the State Special Protection Agency. For trips to the countryside, either Toyota Land Cruiser Series 200 or Lexus LX570 are used.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Montenegro">Montenegro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Montenegro">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Montenegro" title="Prime Minister of Montenegro">Prime Minister of Montenegro</a> and senior state officials of <a href="/wiki/Montenegro" title="Montenegro">Montenegro</a> use a fleet of <a href="/wiki/Audi" title="Audi">Audi</a> limousines, notably the <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a> models, and lower ranked officials travel in <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_E-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz E-Class">Mercedes-Benz E-Class</a> models. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_M-Class" title="Mercedes M-Class">Mercedes M-Class</a>, <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Passat" title="Volkswagen Passat">Volkswagen Passat</a> are also seen. They are escorted by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_5" title="BMW 5">BMW 5s</a>, and additional police <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_A-class" title="Mercedes A-class">Mercedes A-class</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/VW_Golf_4" title="VW Golf 4">VW Golf 4</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/VW_Golf_5" title="VW Golf 5">VW Golf 5</a></p>
<p>The first state vehicles were a fleet of vehicles, unknown by model names, probably from Austria-Hungary, Germany, France, Russia and the United Kingdom. They were bought in the period 1908–1910 and most are seen in a <a class="external text" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9n7oIEznMts" rel="nofollow">1910 Coronation video from an archive</a> where Knyaz <a href="/wiki/Nikola_I_Petrovi%C4%87-Njego%C5%A1" title="Nikola I Petrović-Njegoš">Nikola I Petrović-Njegoš</a> was proclaimed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/King_of_Montenegro" title="King of Montenegro">King of Montenegro</a></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nepal">Nepal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Nepal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Nepal" title="President of Nepal">President of Nepal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bidhya_Devi_Bhandari" title="Bidhya Devi Bhandari">Bidhya Devi Bhandari</a> uses a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz" title="Mercedes Benz">Mercedes Benz</a> <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_E-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz E-Class">E-Class W210 Bullet Proof Car</a> for her daily transport, while the Nepalese state car is an armoured stretched <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_XJ" title="Jaguar XJ">Jaguar XJ</a>. The former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Nepal" title="Prime Minister of Nepal">Prime Minister of Nepal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Baburam_Bhattarai" title="Baburam Bhattarai">Baburam Bhattarai</a> used a Nepali-made <a href="/wiki/Hulas_Motors" title="Hulas Motors">Mustang bullet proof Max</a> four-wheel drive. All the State Cars in Nepal are international standard giving all the facilities.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Netherlands">Netherlands</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Netherlands">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dutch_Royal_Family">Dutch Royal Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=73" title="Edit section: Dutch Royal Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The first car to be owned by the Dutch <a href="/wiki/Monarchy_of_the_Netherlands" title="Monarchy of the Netherlands">royal family</a> was a 1908 <a href="/wiki/Renault" title="Renault">Renault</a>, purchased by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hendrik_of_Mecklenburg-Schwerin" title="Hendrik of Mecklenburg-Schwerin">Prince Hendrik</a>. In the years that followed, it would be joined by nine royal limousines from the Amsterdam carriage maker <a href="/wiki/Spyker" title="Spyker">Spijker</a>. Between 1925 and the late 1950s, the royal limousines were supplied by <a href="/wiki/Cadillac" title="Cadillac">Cadillac</a>, after which the royal household switched to the <a href="/wiki/Ford_Motor_Company" title="Ford Motor Company">Ford Motor Company</a>. However, in 1957 a customized <a href="/wiki/Royal_Dutch_State_Limousine" title="Royal Dutch State Limousine">Rolls-Royce Silver Wraith</a> was commissioned by <a href="/wiki/Juliana_of_the_Netherlands" title="Juliana of the Netherlands">Queen Juliana</a> and delivered in 1958.</p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hofauto.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="800" data-file-width="1200" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Hofauto.jpg/220px-Hofauto.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Hofauto.jpg/330px-Hofauto.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Hofauto.jpg/440px-Hofauto.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hofauto.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Volvo S80, used by Dutch King Willem Alexander.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The current official royal limousine is a custom built stretched <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a>L model, to be used by <a href="/wiki/Willem-Alexander_of_the_Netherlands" title="Willem-Alexander of the Netherlands">King Willem Alexander</a>. This stretched A8L is 45 cm longer compared to the normal A8L.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64"><a href="#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup> A custom built stretch <a href="/wiki/Volvo_S80" title="Volvo S80">Volvo S80</a> limousine is still being used by the former <a href="/wiki/Beatrix_of_the_Netherlands" title="Beatrix of the Netherlands">Queen Beatrix</a>. Other members of the royal family use different cars. Visiting <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Head_of_State" title="Head of State">heads of state</a> are chauffeured in a stretched and armoured <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_DTS" title="Cadillac DTS">Cadillac DTS</a> which replaced the 20-year-old <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Town_Car" title="Lincoln Town Car">Lincoln Town Car</a>.</p>
<p>Other cars are a few non-stretched Volvo S80s and a V70, Audi A6 and A8 and <a href="/wiki/Ford_Focus" title="Ford Focus">Ford Focus</a>, Mondeo and Galaxy for the royal household. The Royal Stables have also a <a href="/wiki/Ford_Scorpio" title="Ford Scorpio">Ford Scorpio</a> <a href="/wiki/Landaulet" title="Landaulet">Landaulet</a>, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_W126" title="Mercedes W126">Mercedes W126</a> 4-door convertible, and a blue coach and a blue <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_Viano" title="Mercedes-Benz Viano">Mercedes-Benz Viano</a> and <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Crafter" title="Volkswagen Crafter">Volkswagen Crafter</a> vip bus. The royal bodyguards drive Audi A6 models.</p>
<p>All royal automobiles are painted in royal-blue, with standard Dutch number plates, as well as a plate beginning with AA, a special designation for the royal household. Other vehicles used by the royal family are Audi or Mercedes. Of course the members of the royal family also have private vehicles for their own use. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/King_Willem-Alexander" title="King Willem-Alexander">King Willem-Alexander</a> has owned a red <a href="/wiki/Volvo_XC90" title="Volvo XC90">Volvo XC90</a>. The late <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prince_Bernhard" title="Prince Bernhard">Prince Bernhard</a>, the former Queen’s father had a collection of Ferraris, and other exotic cars.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dutch_government">Dutch government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: Dutch government">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_Netherlands" title="Prime Minister of the Netherlands">Prime Minister of the Netherlands</a> uses an armoured <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a> and sometimes an <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a>. Previously, an armoured <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_7-Series" title="BMW 7-Series">BMW 7-Series</a> was used. Both cars are owned by the Royal and Diplomatic Security Service (DKDB).</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Zealand">New Zealand</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=75" title="Edit section: New Zealand">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Governor-General_of_New_Zealand_Jaguar_XJ8_Battle_of_Britain_70th_commemorations.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1065" data-file-width="1600" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Governor-General_of_New_Zealand_Jaguar_XJ8_Battle_of_Britain_70th_commemorations.jpg/220px-Governor-General_of_New_Zealand_Jaguar_XJ8_Battle_of_Britain_70th_commemorations.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Governor-General_of_New_Zealand_Jaguar_XJ8_Battle_of_Britain_70th_commemorations.jpg/330px-Governor-General_of_New_Zealand_Jaguar_XJ8_Battle_of_Britain_70th_commemorations.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Governor-General_of_New_Zealand_Jaguar_XJ8_Battle_of_Britain_70th_commemorations.jpg/440px-Governor-General_of_New_Zealand_Jaguar_XJ8_Battle_of_Britain_70th_commemorations.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Governor-General_of_New_Zealand_Jaguar_XJ8_Battle_of_Britain_70th_commemorations.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The official vehicle of the Governor-General of New Zealand in 2010.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Governor-General_of_New_Zealand" title="Governor-General of New Zealand">Governor-General</a> travels in a <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series_(F01)" title="BMW 7 Series (F01)">Long wheel base BMW 7 Series (F02)</a>. Although this vehicle has been debadged, it is most likely a 730Ld as are all other state BMWs. However while all other state BMWs are Silver, the Governor-General's BMW is black. Between 1996 to 2011, the Governor General used a <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_XJ" title="Jaguar XJ">Jaguar XJ Sovereign</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup> Before 1996, he or she traveled in a <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_VI" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom VI">Rolls-Royce Phantom VI</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66"><a href="#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup> During official travel it is the only vehicle in the country not required to use standard number plates.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup> The official flag of the Governor General is flown on the car in which he/she is travelling. The Queen of New Zealand, <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">Elizabeth II</a>, has her own flag, which is used when she is travelling in the country, but there are no specific cars reserved for her use.</p>
<p>From the 1960s up until 2011, The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_New_Zealand" title="Prime Minister of New Zealand">Prime Minister</a> used to travel in one of two cars, one being a <a href="/wiki/Holden_Caprice" title="Holden Caprice">Holden Statesman/Caprice</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sedan_(car)" title="Sedan (car)">sedan</a> or <a href="/wiki/Ford_Fairlane_(Australia)" title="Ford Fairlane (Australia)">Ford Fairlane</a>, usually followed by the other vehicle containing their security detail. The Prime Minister's <a href="/wiki/Wellington" title="Wellington">Wellington</a>-based car has the number plate CR1, and all other cars in the fleet for Ministers have number plates starting in the CR series. The main motorcade vehicles consist of <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Highlander" title="Toyota Highlander">Toyota Highlanders</a> operated by the <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_Police" title="New Zealand Police">New Zealand Police</a> <a href="/wiki/Diplomatic_Protection_Service" title="Diplomatic Protection Service">Diplomatic Protection Service</a>. The estimated purchase price per unit is NZ$69,900<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup> In 2011 the Government upgraded the ministerial fleet with 34 new BMW F02 730Ld limousines.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TVNZ_4029069_70-0"><a href="#cite_note-TVNZ_4029069-70">[70]</a></sup> The retiring fleet was kept on for use during the <a href="/wiki/2011_Rugby_World_Cup" title="2011 Rugby World Cup">2011 Rugby World Cup</a>. In October 2014 it was announced the BMW limousines were to be replaced,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71"><a href="#cite_note-71">[71]</a></sup> however many of the 2011 Models remain in service. The Prime Minister still uses a 2011 model, even though other ministers use 2014 models.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nicaragua">Nicaragua</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=76" title="Edit section: Nicaragua">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The President of <a href="/wiki/Nicaragua" title="Nicaragua">Nicaragua</a> uses a <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_G-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz G-Class">Mercedes-Benz G-Class</a>. In the past, the <a href="/wiki/Somoza_family" title="Somoza family">Somoza family</a> used several luxury cars during their 43 years in the presidency. A <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W189" title="Mercedes-Benz W189">Mercedes-Benz Type 300</a> was used for official ceremonies. Others were <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz" title="Mercedes-Benz">Mercedes-Benz</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cadillac" title="Cadillac">Cadillac</a> limousines.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nigeria">Nigeria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=77" title="Edit section: Nigeria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Nigeria" title="President of Nigeria">President of Nigeria</a> and other high-profile government officials use a black armored Mercedes Benz S-Class 2012 adorned with the Nigerian flag and official party flag. Other luxury cars, like the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E66" title="BMW E66">BMW 730Ld</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Range_Rover" title="Range Rover">Range Rover</a>, all armoured, are used. The President travels in a motorcade of 30 cars and ten escort motorcycles, along with police cars and 6 Mercedes S-550 of SSS surrounding the president's car. Foreign visitors also travel along in the president's car.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="North_Korea">North Korea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: North Korea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In North Korea (DPRK), most frequently used for state events are the <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_600" title="Mercedes-Benz 600">Mercedes-Benz 600 Landaulets</a>. DPRK owns two, originally bought by <a href="/wiki/Kim_Il-sung" title="Kim Il-sung">Kim Il-sung</a> (the Great Leader) in the late 1960s, but also used occasionally by both <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-il" title="Kim Jong-il">Kim Jong-il</a> (the Dear Leader) and <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-un" title="Kim Jong-un">Kim Jong-un</a> (usually now styled the Supreme Leader). Daimler-Benz made fifty-nine 600 Landaulets, twelve with a longer convertible roof which (while not an official factory designation) are usually referred to as <i>presidential landaulets</i>. Both the DPRK's 600s have the longer roof.</p>
<p>Besides Mercedes-Benz 600, Kim Jong-un is also reportedly using the <a href="/wiki/Range_Rover_(L322)" title="Range Rover (L322)">Range Rover Supercharged</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72"><a href="#cite_note-72">[72]</a></sup></p>
<p>In addition, North Korean government officials are also known to drive various Audi, Mercedes and Lexus vehicles, mainly the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Audi_A6L" title="Audi A6L">Audi A6L</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_E-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz E-Class">Mercedes-Benz E-Class</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Lexus_GS" title="Lexus GS">Lexus GS</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Norway">Norway</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=79" title="Edit section: Norway">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The King and Queen uses a 2016 <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8 L</a> Extended (known as A2) for formal use, and a streched Mercedes E-Class (Binz Business) (known as A7) as HM Queen's private limousine. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Norwegian_monarchy" title="Norwegian monarchy">Crown Prince and Crown Princess</a>, uses a <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS_(XF40)" title="Lexus LS (XF40)">Lexus LS 600h</a> limousine, acquired in early 2008.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73"><a href="#cite_note-73">[73]</a></sup> The Royal Family of <a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norway</a> also uses a 2007 <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a>, an E65 and an E67 <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a>, an vintage 1966 <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Continental" title="Lincoln Continental">Lincoln Continental</a> convertibal (A5), a couple of stretched <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cadillac_Deville" title="Cadillac Deville">Cadillac Deville (Superior Commercial Glass)</a> and a couple of stretched <a href="/wiki/Volvo_S80" title="Volvo S80">Volvo S80 (Nilsson)</a>. The BMWs are often driven by the <a href="/wiki/Harald_V_of_Norway" title="Harald V of Norway">King</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Queen_of_Norway" title="Queen of Norway">Queen</a>.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Norway" title="Prime Minister of Norway">Prime Minister of Norway</a> uses an armoured 2015 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S600" title="Mercedes S600">Mercedes S600 L.</a> The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Norway" title="Prime Minister of Norway">Prime Minister of Norway</a> are escorted by <a href="/wiki/BMW_X5_(E70)" title="BMW X5 (E70)">BMW X5s</a> driven by agents of the <a href="/wiki/Office_of_the_Prime_Minister_(Norway)" title="Office of the Prime Minister (Norway)">SMK</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Norwegian_Police_Service" title="Norwegian Police Service">Norwegian Police Service</a>.</p>
<p>Various governmental ministers are transported in an <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes S-class</a> or a <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7-series</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Oman">Oman</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=80" title="Edit section: Oman">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sultan_Qaboos" title="Sultan Qaboos">Sultan Qaboos</a> drives around the country in the following cars:</p>
<ul>
