<li>2 Maroon colored 2007 model <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S-Class" title="Mercedes S-Class">Mercedes S-Class</a> pullman.</li>
<li>4 Red colored 2003 model <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S600" title="Mercedes S600">Mercedes S600</a> pullman.</li>
<li>4 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maybach_62" title="Maybach 62">Maybach 62</a></li>
</ul>
<p>In addition to this, his garage contains:</p>
<ul>
<li>Several <a href="/wiki/List_of_Rolls-Royce_motor_cars" title="List of Rolls-Royce motor cars">Rolls-Royces</a></li>
<li>A line of <a href="/wiki/Lamborghini" title="Lamborghini">Lamborghinis</a></li>
<li>A couple of <a href="/wiki/Ferrari" title="Ferrari">Ferraris</a>, <a href="/wiki/Street_%26_Racing_Technology" title="Street &amp; Racing Technology">SRTs</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aston_Martin" title="Aston Martin">Aston Martins</a></li>
<li>More than 20 <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz" title="Mercedes-Benz">Mercedes</a></li>
<li>Up to 10 <a href="/wiki/BMW" title="BMW">BMWs</a></li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Pakistan">Pakistan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Pakistan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Pakistan" title="President of Pakistan">President</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Pakistan" title="Prime Minister of Pakistan">Prime Minister of Pakistan</a> both have <a href="/wiki/Armored_car_(VIP)" title="Armored car (VIP)">armoured</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W222" title="Mercedes-Benz W222">Mercedes-Benz W222</a> cars. Both the PM and the President travel in a motorcade with up to seven decoy components, each component exactly identical – one traffic police car escorting the flag-bearing armored Mercedes followed by a Toyota Land Cruiser with electronic jamming devices, and two other Land Cruisers of guards. The head and tail of the overall motorcade is usually protected by many rapid response police vehicles. The motorcade is escorted by at least half a dozen traffic motorbikes, and is trailed by a military ambulance and a firefighting truck. When the PM and President travel out of city, the motorcades are additionally escorted by further vehicles of the local police. The convoy comprises 20 to 100 vehicles, depending on the location and destination.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Pakistan" title="Government of Pakistan">government of Pakistan</a> has also arranged for armoured cars equipped with jamming devices for the <a href="/wiki/Chairman_of_the_Senate_of_Pakistan" title="Chairman of the Senate of Pakistan">Senate Chairman</a> and <a href="/wiki/Speaker_of_the_National_Assembly_of_Pakistan" title="Speaker of the National Assembly of Pakistan">Speaker of the National Assembly</a>. The Pakistan Foreign Ministry also operates up to 10 of these identical armoured cars which are used to transport VIPs and visiting heads of state. Politicians are also seen in Toyota Land Cruisers. Former Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Benazir_Bhutto" title="Benazir Bhutto">Benazir Bhutto</a> was assassinated in a Toyota Land Cruiser while campaigning for re-election.</p>
<p>Latest reports suggest that the Prime Minister, <a href="/wiki/Nawaz_Sharif" title="Nawaz Sharif">Nawaz Sharif</a> has recently acquired two BMW 760Li High Security sedans, which cost PKR 119.742 million and PKR 124.995 million respectively. The Cabinet Division’s Central Pool of Car (CPC), BMW 750Li High Security and 760Li High Security. Both of them were certified with BRV 2009 and VR7 ballistics protection. The non-transparent sections have been certified as having VR9 levels of protection. This is the first set of cars to be granted such high levels of security. It included undercarriage Armour, 6 cm safety glazing at multi-layer laminated glass it was told that the import duties and taxes had been exempted from the price of the cars.</p>
<p>Pakistan's Members of the National Assembly have government maintained <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Corolla" title="Toyota Corolla">Toyota Corollas</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Panama">Panama</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: Panama">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_Panama" title="President of Panama">President of Panama</a> uses a black armored <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Suburban" title="Chevrolet Suburban">Chevrolet Suburban</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Ford_Explorer" title="Ford Explorer">Ford Explorer</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Land_Cruiser" title="Toyota Land Cruiser">Toyota Land Cruiser</a> are use for the Institutional Protection Service (S.P.I.) as escort presidential motorcade and 400cc motorcycles. High-security motorcades may include up to ten vehicles.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Peru">Peru</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: Peru">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hongqi_H7.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="169" data-file-width="382" height="97" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Hongqi_H7.jpg/220px-Hongqi_H7.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Hongqi_H7.jpg/330px-Hongqi_H7.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/4/47/Hongqi_H7.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hongqi_H7.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Peruvian Official State Car</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Peru" title="President of Peru">President of Peru</a> is driven in a black armored Lexus LS 460hL. In May 2015, the Lexus was chosen by the president Humala as the official brand of the Government of Peru.</p>
<p>Before used a black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_S600" title="Mercedes Benz S600">Mercedes Benz S600</a> and also a black armored <a href="/wiki/Hongqi_(marque)" title="Hongqi (marque)">Hongqi</a> (Red Flag) <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Crown_Majesta#Fourth-generation_series_S180" title="Toyota Crown Majesta">HQ430</a> which was donated by China.</p>
<p>The Prime Minister of Peru and the other Ministers are driven in Lexus.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Philippines">Philippines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=84" title="Edit section: Philippines">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:The_Philippine_Presidential_Car.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="284" data-file-width="442" height="141" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/The_Philippine_Presidential_Car.jpg/220px-The_Philippine_Presidential_Car.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/The_Philippine_Presidential_Car.jpg/330px-The_Philippine_Presidential_Car.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/The_Philippine_Presidential_Car.jpg/440px-The_Philippine_Presidential_Car.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:The_Philippine_Presidential_Car.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Presidential car of the Philippines, with license plate number "1" and the national flag and presidential standard of the Philippines.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Philippines" title="President of the Philippines">President of the Philippines</a> uses two black, bulletproof <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_W221" title="Mercedes Benz W221">Mercedes Benz W221</a>. When travelling in a motorcade or convoy, the President is always escorted by the <a href="/wiki/Presidential_Security_Group" title="Presidential Security Group">Presidential Security Group</a> in a number of black <a href="/wiki/Nissan_Patrol" title="Nissan Patrol">Nissan Patrol</a>. These high-security motorcades involve as many as 25 vehicles, but the actual number is dependent on the destination.</p>
<p>Presidential cars are registered and bear the <a href="/wiki/Vehicle_registration_plates_of_the_Philippines" title="Vehicle registration plates of the Philippines">licence plate</a> number "1", while the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_the_Philippines" title="Flag of the Philippines">National Flag</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_the_President_of_the_Philippines" title="Flag of the President of the Philippines">Presidential Standard</a> are mounted on the bonnet. Occasionally, the President boards a <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Coaster" title="Toyota Coaster">Toyota Coaster</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mitsubishi_Rosa" title="Mitsubishi Rosa">Mitsubishi Rosa</a> or <a href="/wiki/Nissan_Civilian" title="Nissan Civilian">Nissan Civilian</a> during provincial trips.</p>
<p>The Presidential convoy may consist of the Presidential Car, a backup car (either a second <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class_(W221)#S_600_Guard_Pullman_.282008.E2.80.932013.29" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class (W221)">Mercedes Benz W221 (S600 Guard)</a> or a <a href="/wiki/Hyundai_Equus" title="Hyundai Equus">Hyundai Equus</a>), five to six black <a href="/wiki/Nissan_Patrol" title="Nissan Patrol">Nissan Patrol</a> vans, two <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Fortuner" title="Toyota Fortuner">Toyota Fortuners</a>, two to four <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Suburban" title="Chevrolet Suburban">Chevrolet Suburbans</a>, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ford_E-150" title="Ford E-150">Ford E-150</a> ambulance, up to four police vehicles (<a href="/wiki/Toyota_Corolla_(E120)" title="Toyota Corolla (E120)">Toyota Corolla Altis</a> or <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Vios" title="Toyota Vios">Toyota Vios</a>) and about eight to a dozen motorcycle escorts.</p>
<p>President <a href="/wiki/Benigno_Aquino_III" title="Benigno Aquino III">Benigno Aquino III</a> prefers to use his personal vehicles (a <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Land_Cruiser" title="Toyota Land Cruiser">Toyota Land Cruiser</a> or <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lexus_LX570" title="Lexus LX570">Lexus LX570</a>) instead of the official fleet, and observes regular traffic rules, such as stopping at a red traffic light. He also does not use sirens when travelling in convoy. His successor, <a href="/wiki/Rodrigo_Duterte" title="Rodrigo Duterte">Rodrigo Duterte</a>, also prefers to utilize his personal pick-up truck as his official presidential vehicle.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74"><a href="#cite_note-74">[74]</a></sup></p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_the_Philippines" title="Vice President of the Philippines">Vice President of the Philippines</a> uses a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_W140" title="Mercedes Benz W140">Mercedes Benz W140</a> S-Class, with almost the same number of vehicles as in the presidential security convoy. The Presidential Security Group is also responsible for the Vice-President's security detail.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75"><a href="#cite_note-75">[75]</a></sup></p>
<p>Commonwealth Pres. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Manuel_Quezon" title="Manuel Quezon">Manuel Quezon</a> used a 1937 <a href="/wiki/Chrysler_Airflow" title="Chrysler Airflow">Chrysler Airflow</a> Custom Imperial CW as the first presidential car. Pres. Jose P. Laurel used a 1942 <a href="/wiki/Packard_180" title="Packard 180">Packard 180</a> limousine. Commonwealth Pres. Sergio Osmeña used a 1941 <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_Series_61" title="Cadillac Series 61">Cadillac Series 61</a>. After the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_Colonial_Period_(Philippines)" title="American Colonial Period (Philippines)">American colonial period</a>, President <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Roxas" title="Manuel Roxas">Manuel Roxas</a> used a 1940 <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_Series_70" title="Cadillac Series 70">Cadillac Fleetwood Series 75</a>, which was also used by his successors. A 1946 <a href="/wiki/Packard_Clipper" title="Packard Clipper">Packard Clipper</a> was used by Vice Presidents <a href="/wiki/Elpidio_Quirino" title="Elpidio Quirino">Elpidio Quirino</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fernando_L%C3%B3pez" title="Fernando López">Fernando López</a>. When Quirino assumed the presidency, he used a 1953 <a href="/wiki/Chrysler_Imperial" title="Chrysler Imperial">Chrysler Imperial</a> limousine, whereas Pres. Ramon <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Magsaysay" title="Magsaysay">Magsaysay</a> used a Cadillac Fisher Fleetwood Series 75. Pres. <a href="/wiki/Ferdinand_Marcos" title="Ferdinand Marcos">Ferdinand Marcos</a> used a Mercedes Benz 600 and a Lincoln Continental Signature Series. Pres. <a href="/wiki/Corazon_Aquino" title="Corazon Aquino">Corazon Aquino</a> used a Mercedes-Benz W124 sedan. Pres. <a href="/wiki/Fidel_Ramos" title="Fidel Ramos">Fidel Ramos</a> used a Mercedes-Benz 500 SEL Guard. Pres. <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Estrada" title="Joseph Estrada">Joseph Estrada</a> used a Mercedes-Benz S600. Pres. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gloria_Macapagal-Arroyo" title="Gloria Macapagal-Arroyo">Gloria Macapagal-Arroyo</a> used a Mercedes-Benz S600 Pullman.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Portugal">Portugal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=85" title="Edit section: Portugal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tmulti tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:204px;max-width:204px">
<div style="clear:both;font-weight:bold;text-align:center;background-color:">Portugal Official State Cars</div>
<div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:202px;max-width:202px">
<div class="thumbimage"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pt_car.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="640" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Pt_car.jpg/200px-Pt_car.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Pt_car.jpg/300px-Pt_car.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Pt_car.jpg/400px-Pt_car.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a></div>
<div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">One of several Portuguese Presidential State Cars, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S600" title="Mercedes S600">Mercedes S600</a>, in <a href="/wiki/Porto" title="Porto">Porto</a>. The license plate reads POR with the 'O' being the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Portugal" title="Flag of Portugal">armillary sphere of Portugal</a> and the PR for 'President of Republic'.</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Portugal" title="President of Portugal">President of Portugal</a> is usually driven in an armoured <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S600" title="Mercedes S600">Mercedes S600</a>, in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E67" title="BMW E67">E67 BMW 760 Li</a> or in a Mercedes-Benz E Class 250 CDI BlueEFFICIENCY.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76"><a href="#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup></p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Portugal" title="Prime Minister of Portugal">Prime Minister of Portugal</a> is driven in a Mercedes-Benz S350 BlueTec, in a Volkswagen Phaeton 5.0 V10 TDI or in an electric car, Nissan Leaf.</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Poland">Poland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=86" title="Edit section: Poland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Poland" title="President of Poland">President of Poland</a> uses an <a href="/wiki/Armour" title="Armour">armoured</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E67" title="BMW E67">E67 BMW 760 Li</a> and <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a>L</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Romania">Romania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=87" title="Edit section: Romania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Romania" title="President of Romania">President of Romania</a> rides in his <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a>, escorted by a motorcade consisting of black <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a> (E60) models.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77"><a href="#cite_note-77">[77]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Russia">Russia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=88" title="Edit section: Russia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Zil-41047.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="334" data-file-width="500" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Zil-41047.jpg/220px-Zil-41047.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Zil-41047.jpg/330px-Zil-41047.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Zil-41047.jpg/440px-Zil-41047.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Zil-41047.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/ZIL-41047" title="ZIL-41047">ZIL-41047</a> Presidential car</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">President of Russia</a> is usually seen in an armoured <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S-Class" title="Mercedes S-Class">Mercedes S-Class</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup> stretched limousine as <a href="/wiki/Presidential_state_car_(Russia)" title="Presidential state car (Russia)">his car</a>. The first such model, a W140 variant, was purchased for <a href="/wiki/Boris_Yeltsin" title="Boris Yeltsin">Boris Yeltsin</a> and has been superseded by a W221 model. The limousine is bulletproof, has solid rubber tires, and carries an array of communications equipment.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79"><a href="#cite_note-79">[79]</a></sup> On state visits, it is airlifted to the destination using an <a href="/wiki/Ilyushin_Il-76" title="Ilyushin Il-76">Il-76</a>.</p>
<p>Historically, presidents Yeltsin and Medvedev were driven in Mercedes-Benz S-Class limousines stretched and armored by the Belgian Carat Duchatelet, while President Putin prefers Mercedes-Benz Guard limousines. For President Medvedev's inauguration a special Carat Duchatelet limousine with raised roof was ordered.</p>
<p>The presidential motorcade will usually be escorted by police motorcycle outriders and a series of support vehicles including, but not limited to, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_G-Class" title="Mercedes G-Class">Mercedes G-Class</a>, Mercedes <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_E-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz E-Class">E-Class</a>, standard <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">S-Class</a> models, Mercedes <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SLK-Class" title="SLK-Class">SLK-Class</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_5-Series" title="BMW 5-Series">BMW 5-Series</a> and <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Transporter_(T5)" title="Volkswagen Transporter (T5)">Volkswagen Caravelle</a>.</p>
<p>Under the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USSR" title="USSR">USSR</a>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/General_Secretary_of_the_Communist_Party_of_the_USSR" title="General Secretary of the Communist Party of the USSR">General Secretary of the Communist Party</a> was always driven in a Soviet-built <a href="/wiki/ZIL-41047" title="ZIL-41047">ZIL-41047</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80"><a href="#cite_note-80">[80]</a></sup> escorted by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chaika_(car)" title="Chaika (car)">Chaika</a> models. Two of the Zil limousines are still maintained in the <a href="/wiki/Kremlin" title="Kremlin">Kremlin</a> garage and occasionally seen in use by the military parades on the <a href="/wiki/Victory_Day_(9_May)" title="Victory Day (9 May)">Day of Victory</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81"><a href="#cite_note-81">[81]</a></sup></p>
<p>A new car, Kortezh, is being rolled out in late 2017 to 2020, as the new Russian made state car.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82"><a href="#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Serbia">Serbia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=89" title="Edit section: Serbia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Serbia" title="President of Serbia">President of Serbia</a> uses an armoured <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W221" title="Mercedes-Benz W221">W221</a> (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W221#S_600_Guard_.282006.E2.80.932013.29" title="Mercedes-Benz W221">S 600 Guard</a>) with B6/B7 resistance level,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup> escorted by two <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_E-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz E-Class">Mercedes-Benz E-Class</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W212" title="Mercedes-Benz W212">W212</a> models.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84"><a href="#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Singapore">Singapore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=90" title="Edit section: Singapore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Singapore_President_Car_2013.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="640" data-file-width="960" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Singapore_President_Car_2013.jpg/220px-Singapore_President_Car_2013.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Singapore_President_Car_2013.jpg/330px-Singapore_President_Car_2013.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Singapore_President_Car_2013.jpg/440px-Singapore_President_Car_2013.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Singapore_President_Car_2013.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Singapore's Presidential car in 2013</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Singapore_Prime_Minister_Car_2014.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="700" data-file-width="1024" height="137" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Singapore_Prime_Minister_Car_2014.jpg/200px-Singapore_Prime_Minister_Car_2014.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Singapore_Prime_Minister_Car_2014.jpg/300px-Singapore_Prime_Minister_Car_2014.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Singapore_Prime_Minister_Car_2014.jpg/400px-Singapore_Prime_Minister_Car_2014.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Singapore_Prime_Minister_Car_2014.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Singapore's Prime Ministerial car in 2014</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Singapore" title="President of Singapore">President of Singapore</a> usually travels in a white <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">2010 Mercedes Benz S350L</a>. When travelling to official events such as the <a href="/wiki/Singapore_National_Day_Parade" title="Singapore National Day Parade">National Day Parade</a>, the car displays the Presidential crest in place of a license plate. Normally, it carries the plate SEP1.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Singapore" title="Prime Minister of Singapore">Prime Minister</a> usually travels in a white <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS" title="Lexus LS">2013 Lexus LS460L</a>. The President, Prime Minister and Speaker of Parliament are the only political appointees to be given official cars. All other ministers of the <a href="/wiki/Cabinet_of_Singapore" title="Cabinet of Singapore">cabinet</a> travel in their personal cars.</p>
<p>The State also maintains a small number of state cars for the transport of visiting dignitaries. These cars carry car plates bearing a single S prefix, following by a single digit and no suffix. (E.g. S1, S2, S3). Some of the cars used include an armoured Audi Security A8 W12, as well as a BMW 750iL.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Slovakia">Slovakia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=91" title="Edit section: Slovakia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Klaus-a-Ga%C5%A1parovi%C4%8D-vyznamen%C3%A1n%C3%AD-Tugendhat2013-26.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Klaus-a-Ga%C5%A1parovi%C4%8D-vyznamen%C3%A1n%C3%AD-Tugendhat2013-26.jpg/220px-Klaus-a-Ga%C5%A1parovi%C4%8D-vyznamen%C3%A1n%C3%AD-Tugendhat2013-26.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Klaus-a-Ga%C5%A1parovi%C4%8D-vyznamen%C3%A1n%C3%AD-Tugendhat2013-26.jpg/330px-Klaus-a-Ga%C5%A1parovi%C4%8D-vyznamen%C3%A1n%C3%AD-Tugendhat2013-26.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Klaus-a-Ga%C5%A1parovi%C4%8D-vyznamen%C3%A1n%C3%AD-Tugendhat2013-26.jpg/440px-Klaus-a-Ga%C5%A1parovi%C4%8D-vyznamen%C3%A1n%C3%AD-Tugendhat2013-26.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Klaus-a-Ga%C5%A1parovi%C4%8D-vyznamen%C3%A1n%C3%AD-Tugendhat2013-26.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
President of Slovakia Mercedes-Benz Pullman</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Slovakia" title="President of Slovakia">President of Slovakia</a> uses various vehicles from the Office for the Protection of Constitutional Officials and Diplomatic Missions which has more than 230 cars for the president, prime minister, ministers and state visits. For state visits the president uses an armored <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_Pullman" title="Mercedes Benz Pullman">Mercedes Benz Pullman</a>, for normal driving one of the 230 cars (armored <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a>, <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Phaeton" title="Volkswagen Phaeton">Volkswagen Phaeton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Range_Rover" title="Range Rover">Range Rover</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_X5" title="BMW X5">BMW X5</a>, <a href="/wiki/%C5%A0koda_Superb" title="Škoda Superb">Škoda Superb</a> and other vehicles.</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Slovenia">Slovenia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=92" title="Edit section: Slovenia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Slovenian president Borut Pahor uses an Audi A8 and Prime Minister Miro Cerar uses a BMW 7 series while their <a class="external text" href="http://www.policija.si/eng/index.php/generalpolicedirectorate/90-security-and-protection-centre" rel="nofollow">security officers</a> use BMWs X5 as protection vehicles. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dz-rs.si/wps/portal/en/Home/ODrzavnemZboru/KdoJeKdo/Predsednik" rel="nofollow">Speaker of Parliament</a> and <a class="external text" href="http://www.vlada.si/en/about_the_government/" rel="nofollow">ministers</a> are mostly driven in Audis A6 or A8 and BMWs 5 series.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Somalia">Somalia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=93" title="Edit section: Somalia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Somalia" title="President of Somalia">President of Somalia</a> is driven in various state-owned armored vehicles. A <a href="/wiki/Nissan_Patrol" title="Nissan Patrol">Nissan Patrol</a> often leads the motorcade, which is guarded by the presidential corps. Instead of a number plate, it features the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Somalia" title="Flag of Somalia">flag of Somalia</a>. A similar vehicle is used by the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Somalia" title="Prime Minister of Somalia">Prime Minister of Somalia</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="South_Africa">South Africa</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=94" title="Edit section: South Africa">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_South_Africa" title="President of South Africa">President of South Africa</a> is driven in an armored <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a> or on occasion a Mercedes-Benz S-Class. A similar car is used by the <a href="/wiki/Deputy_President_of_South_Africa" title="Deputy President of South Africa">Deputy President of South Africa</a>.</p>
<p>The presidential motorcade is composed of numerous <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=GOLF_7R&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="GOLF 7R (page does not exist)">GOLF 7R</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jeep_Grand_Cherokee" title="Jeep Grand Cherokee">Jeep Grand Cherokee</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_3_series" title="BMW 3 series">BMW 3 series</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_ML-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz ML-Class">Mercedes-Benz ML-Class</a> models, followed by a number of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_V-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz V-Class">Mercedes-Benz V-Class</a> and police cars.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="South_Korea">South Korea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=95" title="Edit section: South Korea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:South_Korean_Presidential_Car_1992_Cadillac.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4940" height="127" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/South_Korean_Presidential_Car_1992_Cadillac.jpg/220px-South_Korean_Presidential_Car_1992_Cadillac.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/South_Korean_Presidential_Car_1992_Cadillac.jpg/330px-South_Korean_Presidential_Car_1992_Cadillac.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/South_Korean_Presidential_Car_1992_Cadillac.jpg/440px-South_Korean_Presidential_Car_1992_Cadillac.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:South_Korean_Presidential_Car_1992_Cadillac.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
1992 <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_Brougham" title="Cadillac Brougham">Cadillac Brougham</a>, the former South Korean Presidential Car.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_South_Korea" title="President of South Korea">President of South Korea</a> often rides in an armored <a href="/wiki/Hyundai_Equus" title="Hyundai Equus">Hyundai Equus VL500(550)</a> <a href="/wiki/Limousine" title="Limousine">limousine</a>, 3 of which were provided in 2009 by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hyundai_Motors" title="Hyundai Motors">Hyundai Motors</a>. These are the first vehicles manufactured in South Korea to be secured from the factory at a level approaching that of <a href="/wiki/BMW" title="BMW">BMW</a> or <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz" title="Mercedes-Benz">Mercedes-Benz</a> factory limousines. The president also uses 2008-model <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W221" title="Mercedes-Benz W221">Mercedes-Benz W221</a> Pullman Guard.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85"><a href="#cite_note-85">[85]</a></sup></p>
<p>Previously, the <a href="/wiki/President_of_South_Korea" title="President of South Korea">President</a> rode in an armoured <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a> <a href="/wiki/Limousine" title="Limousine">limousine</a> which was purchased in 2005. Before that a 2002-model <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W220" title="Mercedes-Benz W220">Mercedes-Benz W220</a> was used, the late president <a href="/wiki/Roh_Moo-hyun" title="Roh Moo-hyun">Roh Moo-hyun</a> used it during peace talks with <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a>. The presidential motorcade is escorted by <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Tahoe" title="Chevrolet Tahoe">Chevrolet Tahoe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Suburban" title="Chevrolet Suburban">Chevrolet Suburban</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ford_Excursion" title="Ford Excursion">Ford Excursion</a>, also with several identical <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W220" title="Mercedes-Benz W220">Mercedes-Benz W220s</a>.</p>
<p>The late president <a href="/wiki/Kim_Dae-jung" title="Kim Dae-jung">Kim Dae-jung</a> used an armored <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E38" title="BMW E38">BMW 740iAL</a>, offered by BMW Korea, for his state visit to <a href="/wiki/Mongolia" title="Mongolia">Mongolia</a> in June 1999.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86"><a href="#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_(South_Korea)" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs (South Korea)">The Ministry of Foreign Affairs</a> keeps an armored <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_DTS" title="Cadillac DTS">Cadillac DTS</a> limousine by <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Alpine_Armoring&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Alpine Armoring (page does not exist)">Alpine Armoring</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87"><a href="#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup> and an armored <a href="/wiki/Hyundai_Equus" title="Hyundai Equus">Hyundai Equus</a> limousine<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup> for foreign dignitaries. Each vehicle was acquired between 2010 and 2011.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Spain">Spain</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=96" title="Edit section: Spain">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Spanish_Royal_Family">Spanish Royal Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=97" title="Edit section: Spanish Royal Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Royal_Family" title="Spanish Royal Family">Spanish Royal Family</a> enjoys one of the largest fleets of cars in Spain. Various armoured vehicles are used by the family, including <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a> models and the exclusive <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_IV" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom IV">Rolls-Royce Phantom IV</a> utilized in ceremonial occasions. Only 18 of the latter were ever built, all being reserved for royalty or heads of state. Three were ordered by the Government of Spain for the use of <a href="/wiki/Francisco_Franco" title="Francisco Franco">General Franco</a> and are now available for use by the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Royal_Family" title="Spanish Royal Family">Spanish Royal Family</a>; they belong to the Spanish Army. One is a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Landaulette" title="Landaulette">landaulette</a> and the other two are limousines. A special order was placed on the marriage of the then-<a href="/wiki/Prince_of_Asturias" title="Prince of Asturias">Prince of Asturias</a> (now King <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Felipe_VI" title="Felipe VI">Felipe VI</a>) when a Phantom IV was rebuilt to include armoured protection. Modifications included heavy-duty air conditioning and a special glazed armoured bubble to protect the rear passengers. The modifications cost over €360,000.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Royal_Family" title="Spanish Royal Family">Spanish Royal Family</a> uses mainly <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S600</a> models for its official transport, with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_5-Series" title="BMW 5-Series">BMW 5-Series</a> (2007–2008) cars as escort vehicles. The motorcade is composed of around 15 cars<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2008)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>. The personal cars of the former King <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Juan_Carlos_I" title="Juan Carlos I">Juan Carlos I</a> are a specially customised <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maybach_57_S" title="Maybach 57 S">Maybach 57 S</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup> and an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Audi_RS6" title="Audi RS6">Audi RS6</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Spanish_government">Spanish government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=98" title="Edit section: Spanish government">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Spain" title="Prime Minister of Spain">Prime Minister of Spain</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/First_Vice_President_of_the_Government_(Spain)" title="First Vice President of the Government (Spain)">Deputy Prime Minister</a> of Spain both use Audi vehicles. The premier's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Audi_A8L" title="Audi A8L">Audi A8L</a> was purchased in March 2005 shortly after retiring the former A8 used by PM <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Aznar" title="José María Aznar">José María Aznar</a>. The vehicle, which then cost the Spanish government well over 380,000 Euros (approx. $520,000 USD), is said to be equipped with the latest features, runflats, <a href="/wiki/EN_1063" title="EN 1063">level B7+ armouring</a>, satellite communications and various special items that are kept secret by the Spanish officials. The fleet has been renovated and now includes various new Audi A8L, Mercedes-Benz S600 and A6s, although former prime minister, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jose_Luis_Rodriguez_Zapatero" title="Jose Luis Rodriguez Zapatero">Jose Luis Rodriguez Zapatero</a> wanted to swap those cars for the hybrid <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Prius" title="Toyota Prius">Toyota Prius</a> to save fuel oil.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sri_Lanka">Sri Lanka</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=99" title="Edit section: Sri Lanka">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Sri_Lanka" title="President of Sri Lanka">President of Sri Lanka</a> is driven in an armored Black <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class_(W221)#S_600_Guard_.282006.E2.80.932013.29" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class (W221)">Mercedes-Benz S-Class (Guard)</a> or armored Black <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E67" title="BMW E67">BMW 7 Series</a> escorted by a selection of marked and unmarked <a href="/wiki/President%27s_Security_Division" title="President's Security Division">President's Security Division</a> vehicles. During official travel it is the only vehicle in the country not required to use standard number plates. The official flag of the President is flown on the car in which he/she is travelling.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Sri_Lanka" title="Prime Minister of Sri Lanka">Prime Minister of Sri Lanka</a> is driven in a Black Mercedes-Benz S-Class (Guard) escorted by <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister%27s_Security_Division" title="Prime Minister's Security Division">Prime Minister's Security Division</a> vehicles. The general practice remains that the out going President will take the vehicles used in his or her term for use in retirement and the incoming President will purchase new ones. Same applies to the Prime Minister if he or she moves on to the post of Leader of the Opposition.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sweden">Sweden</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=100" title="Edit section: Sweden">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Estpresident_1c300_8576.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3744" data-file-width="5616" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/Estpresident_1c300_8576.jpg/220px-Estpresident_1c300_8576.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/Estpresident_1c300_8576.jpg/330px-Estpresident_1c300_8576.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/Estpresident_1c300_8576.jpg/440px-Estpresident_1c300_8576.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Estpresident_1c300_8576.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The King of Sweden and the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Estonia" title="President of Estonia">President of Estonia</a> in a <a href="/wiki/Daimler_DS420" title="Daimler DS420">Daimler DS420</a> on the latter's state visit to Sweden in 2011.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The current official car of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/King_of_Sweden" title="King of Sweden">King of Sweden</a> is a stretched <a href="/wiki/Volvo_S80" title="Volvo S80">Volvo S80</a>, escorted by the <a href="/wiki/Swedish_Security_Service" title="Swedish Security Service">Swedish Security Service</a> in <a href="/wiki/BMW_X5" title="BMW X5">BMW X5</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_5-Series" title="BMW 5-Series">BMW 5-Series</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_E-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz E-Class">Mercedes-Benz E-Class</a> models. For official occasions like state visits there is an <a href="/wiki/Daimler_DS420" title="Daimler DS420">Daimler DS420</a>. There are also a number of different cars in the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Stables_(Sweden)" title="Royal Stables (Sweden)">Royal Stables</a>, which are used on special occasions. The first royal motor car in Sweden was a <a href="/wiki/Daimler_Company" title="Daimler Company">Daimler</a> bought in 1899 for <a href="/wiki/Gustaf_V_of_Sweden" title="Gustaf V of Sweden">Crown Prince Gustaf</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup></p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Sweden" title="Prime Minister of Sweden">Prime Minister of Sweden</a> and other Cabinet Ministers are chauffeured around in an armored <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E67" title="BMW E67">BMW 7 Series</a> and several <a href="/wiki/BMW_X5" title="BMW X5">BMW X5</a>s, also escorted by the <a href="/wiki/Swedish_Security_Service" title="Swedish Security Service">Swedish Security Service</a>.</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Taiwan">Taiwan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=101" title="Edit section: Taiwan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Taiwan_motorcade_pic.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3000" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Taiwan_motorcade_pic.jpg/220px-Taiwan_motorcade_pic.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Taiwan_motorcade_pic.jpg/330px-Taiwan_motorcade_pic.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Taiwan_motorcade_pic.jpg/440px-Taiwan_motorcade_pic.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Taiwan_motorcade_pic.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Taiwanese Presidential motorcade</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Republic_of_China" title="President of the Republic of China">President of the Republic of China</a> has historically travelled in <a href="/wiki/Cadillac" title="Cadillac">Cadillac</a> sedans, reflecting the ROC's close relations with the United States. Former President <a href="/wiki/Chiang_Kai-shek" title="Chiang Kai-shek">Chiang Kai-shek</a>'s two armored Cadillacs are on exhibition in the <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Memorial" title="Lincoln Memorial">Lincoln Memorial</a>-like National <a href="/wiki/Chiang_Kai-shek_Memorial_Hall" title="Chiang Kai-shek Memorial Hall">Chiang Kai-shek Memorial Hall</a> in the capital city of <a href="/wiki/Taipei" title="Taipei">Taipei</a>.</p>
<p>Former President <a href="/wiki/Chen_Shui-bian" title="Chen Shui-bian">Chen Shui-bian</a> discontinued the use of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cadillac_DeVille" title="Cadillac DeVille">Cadillac DeVille</a>, preferring a Lincoln in his first term and a BMW 7-Series in his second term. Former president <a href="/wiki/Ma_Ying-jeou" title="Ma Ying-jeou">Ma Ying-jeou</a> used four BMW F03 750Lis, usually escorted by two BMW R1200RTs police bikes, one BMW E65 750i, and two BMW F10 5-Series police cars (one at the front and one at the end).</p>
<p>From 2016, current president <a href="/wiki/Tsai_Ing-wen" title="Tsai Ing-wen">Tsai Ing-wen</a> uses a <a href="/wiki/Audi_A8" title="Audi A8">Audi A8 L Security</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92"><a href="#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Thailand">Thailand</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=102" title="Edit section: Thailand">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Thai_Royal_family">Thai Royal family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=103" title="Edit section: Thai Royal family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Maybach62.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2783" data-file-width="3872" height="158" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Maybach62.jpg/220px-Maybach62.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Maybach62.jpg/330px-Maybach62.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Maybach62.jpg/440px-Maybach62.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Maybach62.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
King <a href="/wiki/Bhumibol_Adulyadej" title="Bhumibol Adulyadej">Bhumibol Adulyadej's</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maybach_62" title="Maybach 62">Maybach 62</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>King <a href="/wiki/Bhumibol_Adulyadej" title="Bhumibol Adulyadej">Bhumibol Adulyadej</a> travels in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maybach_62" title="Maybach 62">Maybach 62</a> with special plates, with police motorcycle outriders, and an escort of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S-Class" title="Mercedes S-Class">Mercedes S-Class</a> (W222) and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_5-Series" title="BMW 5-Series">BMW 5-Series</a> (F10) police cars. He usually travels in different cars. Most of them are <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S-Class" title="Mercedes S-Class">Mercedes S-Class</a> (W222). The other models including Rolls-Royce Phantom VI, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Silver_Spur" title="Rolls-Royce Silver Spur">Rolls-Royce Silver Spur</a> stretch limousine, Rolls-Royce Silver Spur Park Ward, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lexus_LS460" title="Lexus LS460">Lexus LS460</a>L, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_7-Series" title="BMW 7-Series">BMW 7-Series</a> (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E38" title="BMW E38">E38</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E65" title="BMW E65">E67</a>), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_5-Series" title="BMW 5-Series">BMW 5-Series</a> (<a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series_(E60)" title="BMW 5 Series (E60)">E60</a>), <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_DTS" title="Cadillac DTS">Cadillac DTS</a> stretch limousine, <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Transporter_(T5)" title="Volkswagen Transporter (T5)">Volkswagen Caravelle</a> T5 TDi, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_E-class" title="Mercedes E-class">Mercedes E55 AMG</a> (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/W211" title="W211">W211</a>). All of the royal cars are ivory coloured.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Queen_Sirikit" title="Queen Sirikit">Queen Sirikit</a> mostly travels by <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_DTS" title="Cadillac DTS">Cadillac DTS</a> stretch limousine and modified <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Transporter_(T4)" title="Volkswagen Transporter (T4)">Volkswagen Caravelle T4 TDi</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>Crown Prince <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maha_Vajiralongkorn" title="Maha Vajiralongkorn">Maha Vajiralongkorn</a> usually travels by Rolls-Royce cars. These Rolls-Royces used to be the king's official cars. The Rolls-Royce collection includes a <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_V" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom V">Rolls-Royce Phantom V</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_VI" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom VI">Rolls-Royce Phantom VI</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Silver_Spur" title="Rolls-Royce Silver Spur">Rolls-Royce Silver Spur</a> stretch limousine.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E0%B8%AA%E0%B8%A1%E0%B9%80%E0%B8%94%E0%B9%87%E0%B8%88%E0%B8%9E%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B0%E0%B9%80%E0%B8%97%E0%B8%9E%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B1%E0%B8%95%E0%B8%99%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B2%E0%B8%8A%E0%B8%AA%E0%B8%B8%E0%B8%94%E0%B8%B2%E0%B8%AF_%E0%B8%AA%E0%B8%A2%E0%B8%B2%E0%B8%A1%E0%B8%9A%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%A1%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B2%E0%B8%8A%E0%B8%81%E0%B8%B8%E0%B8%A1%E0%B8%B2%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B5_%E0%B8%9B%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B0%E0%B8%AA%E0%B8%81%E0%B8%99%E0%B8%B4%E0%B8%81%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%82%E0%B8%AD_-_Flickr_-_Abhisit_Vejjajiva.jpg"><img
