2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:%E0%B8%AA%E0%B8%A1%E0%B9%80%E0%B8%94%E0%B9%87%E0%B8%88%E0%B8%9E%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B0%E0%B9%80%E0%B8%97%E0%B8%9E%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B1%E0%B8%95%E0%B8%99%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B2%E0%B8%8A%E0%B8%AA%E0%B8%B8%E0%B8%94%E0%B8%B2%E0%B8%AF_%E0%B8%AA%E0%B8%A2%E0%B8%B2%E0%B8%A1%E0%B8%9A%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%A1%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B2%E0%B8%8A%E0%B8%81%E0%B8%B8%E0%B8%A1%E0%B8%B2%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B5_%E0%B8%9B%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%B0%E0%B8%AA%E0%B8%81%E0%B8%99%E0%B8%B4%E0%B8%81%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%82%E0%B8%AD_-_Flickr_-_Abhisit_Vejjajiva.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Princess_Maha_Chakri_Sirindhorn" title="Princess Maha Chakri Sirindhorn">Princess Maha Chakri Sirindhorn</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E65" title="BMW E65">BMW E67</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Princess_Maha_Chakri_Sirindhorn" title="Princess Maha Chakri Sirindhorn">Princess Maha Chakri Sirindhorn</a> usually travels by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_E66" title="BMW E66">BMW 760Li</a> (E667), <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS_(XF40)" title="Lexus LS (XF40)">Lexus LS600hL</a>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S-Class" title="Mercedes S-Class">Mercedes S-Class</a> (W221 &amp; W222). For unofficial royal journeys she travels in modified <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Viano" title="Mercedes Viano">Mercedes Viano</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>Other royal family members mostly travel by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S-Class" title="Mercedes S-Class">Mercedes S-Class</a> (W221 and W222), ivory colored, for official journeys, with motorcycle escort. A tourist during the early 1990s has confirmed that a mid-1980s Chevrolet Suburban (presumably a 1985 model) is used by the security detail of the Crown Prince.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>Crown Prince <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maha_Vajiralongkorn" title="Maha Vajiralongkorn">Maha Vajiralongkorn</a> has a large collection of cars, including many classic models. Many vehicles formerly belonged to the king, and a few modern cars such as <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz" title="Mercedes-Benz">Mercedes-Benz</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW" title="BMW">BMW</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Cadillac" title="Cadillac">Cadillac</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:2002_Volkswagen_New_Beetle_(9C_MY02.5)_2.0_coupe_(2010-10-01)_01.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1986" data-file-width="3708" height="118" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/2002_Volkswagen_New_Beetle_%289C_MY02.5%29_2.0_coupe_%282010-10-01%29_01.jpg/220px-2002_Volkswagen_New_Beetle_%289C_MY02.5%29_2.0_coupe_%282010-10-01%29_01.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/2002_Volkswagen_New_Beetle_%289C_MY02.5%29_2.0_coupe_%282010-10-01%29_01.jpg/330px-2002_Volkswagen_New_Beetle_%289C_MY02.5%29_2.0_coupe_%282010-10-01%29_01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/2002_Volkswagen_New_Beetle_%289C_MY02.5%29_2.0_coupe_%282010-10-01%29_01.jpg/440px-2002_Volkswagen_New_Beetle_%289C_MY02.5%29_2.0_coupe_%282010-10-01%29_01.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:2002_Volkswagen_New_Beetle_(9C_MY02.5)_2.0_coupe_(2010-10-01)_01.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_New_Beetle" title="Volkswagen New Beetle">Volkswagen New Beetle</a>, similar to the one used by Princess Bajarakitiyabha</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Princess Bajarakitiyabha sometimes drives herself in a red <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mini_Cooper_S" title="Mini Cooper S">Mini Cooper S</a> and a lime-green <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_New_Beetle" title="Volkswagen New Beetle">Volkswagen New Beetle</a> with the motorcade.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>There are also royal cars in convertible form for royal ceremonies, such as a <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Corniche" title="Rolls-Royce Corniche">Rolls-Royce Corniche</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_DTS" title="Cadillac DTS">Cadillac DTS</a> (the hard top was transformed into a convertible top).<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>On official royal journeys, there are a group of more than 45 cars in the motorcade including: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S-Class" title="Mercedes S-Class">Mercedes S-Class</a> (W220, W221, and W222), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_E-class" title="Mercedes E-class">Mercedes E-class</a> (W210 and W211), <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a> (E38), <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a> (E39 and E60), and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S-Class" title="Mercedes S-Class">Mercedes S-Class</a> (W221-W222), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Vito" title="Mercedes Vito">Mercedes Vito</a>, and <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a> used as police cars in ivory color.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>For unofficial royal journeys, the cars in the motorcade are a group of about 15 cars including: <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a> (E38), <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a> (E39 and E60), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S-Class" title="Mercedes S-Class">Mercedes S-Class</a> (W221 and W222), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_E-class" title="Mercedes E-class">Mercedes E-class</a> (W210 and W211) <a href="/wiki/Honda_Accord" title="Honda Accord">Honda Accord</a> <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Camry" title="Toyota Camry">Toyota Camry</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Nissan_Teana" title="Nissan Teana">Nissan Teana</a>. These cars are all ivory coloured.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>The Bureau of The Royal Household also has its own vehicles. These cars are mostly <a href="/wiki/Nissan_Teana" title="Nissan Teana">Nissan Teana</a>, <a href="/wiki/BMW_5_Series" title="BMW 5 Series">BMW 5 Series</a> (E39 and E60), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S-Class" title="Mercedes S-Class">Mercedes S-Class</a> (W220, W221, and W222) and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_E-Class" title="Mercedes E-Class">Mercedes E-Class</a> (W210 and W211). These cars are painted in ivory.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>The royal department has several type of cars, <a href="/wiki/Honda_City" title="Honda City">Honda City V+</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Corolla_(E170)" title="Toyota Corolla (E170)">Toyota Corolla Altis 1.6G</a>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Toyota_Aurion_(XV50)" title="Toyota Aurion (XV50)">Toyota Camry 2.0G</a>. Mostly they are painted white, with the registration plate beginning with ดส-xxxx BKK.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Thai_Prime_Minister">Thai Prime Minister</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=104" title="Edit section: Thai Prime Minister">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In March 2016, Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Prayut_Chan-o-cha" title="Prayut Chan-o-cha">Prayut Chan-o-cha</a> was the recipient of two new armoured Mercedes-Benz S600 Guard sedans, worth 19.5 million baht each. They were among four new luxury armoured cars, costing 78 million baht total, procured by the Secretariat of the Prime Minister. One was equipped with licence plate 4 Kor Dor 29 (4กต 29), the other with 4 Kor Tor 29 (4กท 29). One will serve as Gen Prayut's car for daily use with one as backup. Another two S600 Guard sedans are reserved for high-profile foreign visitors. Gen Prayut's position entitles him to an armored van, which he sometimes uses.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93"><a href="#cite_note-93">[93]</a></sup> He travels by <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Transporter_(T5)" title="Volkswagen Transporter (T5)">Volkswagen Caravelle</a> on some occasions.</p>
<p>Thai ministers mostly travel in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_S-Class" title="Mercedes S-Class">Mercedes S-Class</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Alphard" title="Toyota Alphard">Toyota Alphard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Transporter_(T5)" title="Volkswagen Transporter (T5)">Volkswagen Caravelle</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_XJ" title="Jaguar XJ">Jaguar XJs</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tonga">Tonga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=105" title="Edit section: Tonga">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>For official travel, the King uses <a href="/wiki/Humber_Pullman" title="Humber Pullman">Humber Pullman</a> with body Landaulette, released in 1949. Previous King <a href="/wiki/George_Tupou_V" title="George Tupou V">George Tupou V</a> traveled around the country in the classic Black Cab <a href="/wiki/Austin_FX4" title="Austin FX4">Austin FX4</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trinidad_and_Tobago">Trinidad and Tobago</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=106" title="Edit section: Trinidad and Tobago">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The President and Prime Minister of Trinidad and Tobago each use a black, armoured, 2008 <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Crown" title="Toyota Crown">Toyota Crown</a>. It carries the license plate with a gold coat of arms for the President and PM-1 for the Prime Minister. Each motorcade also includes a decoy car, two police motorcycles, two 2008 Toyota Land Cruisers as support vehicles and a leading <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Camry" title="Toyota Camry">Toyota Camry</a> police vehicle.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94"><a href="#cite_note-94">[94]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Turkey">Turkey</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=107" title="Edit section: Turkey">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:President_Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan_-_Victory_Day_Turkey_2014.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="667" data-file-width="917" height="160" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/President_Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan_-_Victory_Day_Turkey_2014.JPG/220px-President_Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan_-_Victory_Day_Turkey_2014.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/President_Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan_-_Victory_Day_Turkey_2014.JPG/330px-President_Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan_-_Victory_Day_Turkey_2014.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/President_Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan_-_Victory_Day_Turkey_2014.JPG/440px-President_Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan_-_Victory_Day_Turkey_2014.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:President_Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan_-_Victory_Day_Turkey_2014.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Turkish president <a href="/wiki/Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan" title="Recep Tayyip Erdoğan">Recep Tayyip Erdoğan</a> greets people from <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_Series_70#1957.E2.80.931958" title="Cadillac Series 70">1957 Cadillac Series 75</a> on <a href="/wiki/Victory_Day" title="Victory Day">Victory Day</a> 2014.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Most senior politicians use Mercedes-Benz automobiles. The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Turkey" title="President of Turkey">President of Turkey</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Turkey" title="Prime Minister of Turkey">Prime Minister of Turkey</a> use <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a> models.</p>
<p>President <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rauf_Denktas" title="Rauf Denktas">Rauf Denktas</a> of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turkish_Republic_of_North_Cyprus" title="Turkish Republic of North Cyprus">Turkish Republic of North Cyprus</a>, had a red <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_7_series" title="BMW 7 series">BMW 750 Li</a> with gold crests replacing the number plate.</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Uganda">Uganda</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=108" title="Edit section: Uganda">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Ugandan Presidents have usually preferred to ride in European cars. Sir Edward Mutesa, first president of Uganda, drove in a 1960s Rolls-Royce. All succeeding ones drove in black Mercedes Benz limousines.</p>
<p>President Yoweri Museveni drove in black Mercedes cross country and 600 SEL stretch Limos up to the mid-1990s. His convoy now consists of a Toyota Landcruiser 200 presidential car. The Presidency has ceremonial cars that include a stretch 600 SEL mercedes, and a white G Wagon. Escorts travel on double cabin pick up trucks and Mitsubishi Pajero models.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ukraine">Ukraine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=109" title="Edit section: Ukraine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Ukraine" title="President of Ukraine">President of Ukraine</a> uses an armoured <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a> and an armoured <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Phaeton" title="Volkswagen Phaeton">Volkswagen Phaeton</a> Model 2011 in a V12 long version, and for the Motorcade armoured <a href="/wiki/Porsche_Cayenne" title="Porsche Cayenne">Porsche Cayenne</a> by <a href="/wiki/Centigon_(company)" title="Centigon (company)">Centigon</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="United_Kingdom">United Kingdom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=110" title="Edit section: United Kingdom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bentley_State_Limousine">Bentley State Limousine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=111" title="Edit section: Bentley State Limousine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Bentley_State_Limousine" title="Bentley State Limousine">Bentley State Limousine</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:State_Bentley_Long_Walk_Crop_1.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/State_Bentley_Long_Walk_Crop_1.JPG/220px-State_Bentley_Long_Walk_Crop_1.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/State_Bentley_Long_Walk_Crop_1.JPG/330px-State_Bentley_Long_Walk_Crop_1.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/State_Bentley_Long_Walk_Crop_1.JPG/440px-State_Bentley_Long_Walk_Crop_1.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:State_Bentley_Long_Walk_Crop_1.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The 2002 <a href="/wiki/Bentley_State_Limousine" title="Bentley State Limousine">Bentley State Limousine</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The British <a href="/wiki/House_of_Windsor" title="House of Windsor">royal family</a> has a long history of bespoke limousines stretching back to <a href="/wiki/Daimler_Company" title="Daimler Company">Daimler</a> models owned by <a href="/wiki/Edward_VII" title="Edward VII">King Edward VII</a>. On state occasions, <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">Queen Elizabeth II</a> usually travels in one of two armoured <a href="/wiki/Bentley_State_Limousine" title="Bentley State Limousine">Bentley State Limousines</a>. Delivered in 2002 to commemorate the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Jubilee_of_Elizabeth_II" title="Golden Jubilee of Elizabeth II">Queen's Golden Jubilee</a>, these custom-built vehicles are based on the <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Arnage" title="Bentley Arnage">Bentley Arnage</a> floorplan, with a twin-turbocharged 6.75 litre <a href="/wiki/V8_engine" title="V8 engine">V8</a> engine that produces 400 horsepower (300 kW) and 616 pound-feet (835 N·m) of <a href="/wiki/Torque" title="Torque">torque</a>, giving a maximum speed of 130 miles per hour (210 km/h). The state <a href="/wiki/Limousine" title="Limousine">limousine</a> is 3 feet (0.91 m) longer than a standard Bentley Arnage, 10 inches (250 mm) taller and 6 inches (150 mm) wider. It is equipped with broad rear-hinged doors that open almost 90 degrees. The car also has opaque rear window panels that can be removed to allow increased visibility when the occupant is attending a public event or installed for increased privacy when required.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95"><a href="#cite_note-95">[95]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96"><a href="#cite_note-96">[96]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_state_cars">Other state cars</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=112" title="Edit section: Other state cars">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Car_Marriage_Kate_Middleton_and_her_father.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1416" data-file-width="2128" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Car_Marriage_Kate_Middleton_and_her_father.jpg/220px-Car_Marriage_Kate_Middleton_and_her_father.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Car_Marriage_Kate_Middleton_and_her_father.jpg/330px-Car_Marriage_Kate_Middleton_and_her_father.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Car_Marriage_Kate_Middleton_and_her_father.jpg/440px-Car_Marriage_Kate_Middleton_and_her_father.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Car_Marriage_Kate_Middleton_and_her_father.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
1977 Rolls-Royce Phantom VI</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Windsor_Castle_4272.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3008" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Windsor_Castle_4272.JPG/220px-Windsor_Castle_4272.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Windsor_Castle_4272.JPG/330px-Windsor_Castle_4272.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Windsor_Castle_4272.JPG/440px-Windsor_Castle_4272.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Windsor_Castle_4272.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
1986 Rolls-Royce Phantom VI</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Royal_Mews" title="Royal Mews">Royal Mews</a> at <a href="/wiki/Buckingham_Palace" title="Buckingham Palace">Buckingham Palace</a> has a rare <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_IV" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom IV">Rolls-Royce Phantom IV</a>, which was purchased by <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">Princess Elizabeth</a> in 1950, and became a state car upon her accession to the throne as Queen Elizabeth II in 1952. There are also two <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_VI" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom VI">Rolls-Royce Phantom VI</a> models, including the bespoke Silver Jubilee Car, with a raised roof for enhanced visibility, presented by the British motor industry in 1977, as well as a standard model from 1986.</p>
<p>The fleet is augmented by two stretched <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_XJ" title="Jaguar XJ">Jaguar XJ</a> limousines, acquired in 2012; sometimes referred to as "semi-state" limousines, these carry registration plates (NGN 1 and NGN 2) and have been adapted with fittings for a bonnet mascot and roof flag. The Jaguars replaced a pair of 1992 <a href="/wiki/Daimler_DS420" title="Daimler DS420">Daimler DS420</a> limousines, which as of 2015 remain in use as backup to the main fleet for state occasions and foreign visits.</p>
<p>There is also a bespoke 2015 <a href="/wiki/Range_Rover" title="Range Rover">Range Rover</a> for parades and other official rides; the Queen and other members of the Royal Family can stand up in the back for good visibility. This is the fourth in a series of 'Royal Review Vehicles' built for the Queen by <a href="/wiki/Land_Rover" title="Land Rover">Land Rover</a> since 1953; it replaces a 2002 model which remains in use as the second royal review vehicle.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97"><a href="#cite_note-97">[97]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98"><a href="#cite_note-98">[98]</a></sup></p>
<p>All these official royal cars are painted claret and black, and have a flagpole on the roof (or bonnet, in the Range Rover's case). As <a href="/wiki/Law_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Law of the United Kingdom">British law</a> in general does not apply to the sovereign, the monarch's State vehicles do not possess registration plates (although the Jaguar and Daimler models do have them, as do the monarch's personal vehicles and those of other members of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_Royal_Family" title="British Royal Family">Royal Family</a>).</p>
<p>The state cars are sometimes used when the Queen is travelling abroad, and they are also made available for visiting heads of state and other members of the Royal Family on official business. One state car (commonly the rarely used Phantom IV model) is usually on display at the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Mews" title="Royal Mews">Royal Mews</a>, <a href="/wiki/Buckingham_Palace" title="Buckingham Palace">Buckingham Palace</a>, where the State vehicles are kept and maintained.</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Former_state_cars">Former state cars</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=113" title="Edit section: Former state cars">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>From the earliest years of the 20th century Daimler were invariably chosen as the monarch's state cars until the accession of Elizabeth II in 1952 (who began to use Rolls-Royce cars). Many of her predecessors' Daimlers are now on display at the royal motor museum, <a href="/wiki/Sandringham_House" title="Sandringham House">Sandringham House</a>.</p>
<p>A 1954 <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_IV" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom IV">Rolls-Royce Phantom IV</a> State <a href="/wiki/Landaulet" title="Landaulet">Landaulet</a> (retired from the working fleet in the 1980s) is now on permanent loan to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sir_Henry_Royce" title="Sir Henry Royce">Sir Henry Royce</a> Memorial Foundation, <a href="/wiki/Paulerspury" title="Paulerspury">Paulerspury</a>; and a pair of 1961 <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_V" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom V">Rolls-Royce Phantom V</a> state cars (retired from the working fleet after the Bentleys were acquired in 2002) can be seen on public display, one in the purpose-built garage aboard the former Royal Yacht <a href="/wiki/HMY_Britannia" title="HMY Britannia">Britannia</a> in Edinburgh (on loan from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bentley_Motors_Ltd" title="Bentley Motors Ltd">Bentley Motors Ltd</a>), and the other at Sandringham.</p>
<p>Among vehicles displayed at <a href="/wiki/British_Motor_Museum" title="British Motor Museum">British Motor Museum</a>, Gaydon are former State Royal Review Vehicles including a 1954 Land Rover and a 1974 Range Rover.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99"><a href="#cite_note-99">[99]</a></sup></p>
<p>A succession of Daimler limousines has been retained at the Mews through the present reign to serve as 'semi-state' or backup vehicles. A pair of 1969 <a href="/wiki/Vanden_Plas_Princess" title="Vanden Plas Princess">Vanden Plas 4-Litre Princess Limousines</a> served alongside the Daimlers from 1972 until the mid-1990s; one (NGN 1) is displayed at <a href="/wiki/Sandringham_House" title="Sandringham House">Sandringham</a>, the other (NGN 2) is at Gaydon.</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Prince_of_Wales">The Prince of Wales</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=114" title="Edit section: The Prince of Wales">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On formal occasions, The <a href="/wiki/Charles,_Prince_of_Wales" title="Charles, Prince of Wales">Prince of Wales</a> is often seen in a claret and black 1962 <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_V" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom V">Rolls-Royce Phantom V</a> former <a href="/wiki/Landaulet" title="Landaulet">Landaulet</a> (registration plate NLT 1), which he inherited from <a href="/wiki/Queen_Elizabeth_The_Queen_Mother" title="Queen Elizabeth The Queen Mother">Queen Elizabeth The Queen Mother</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Pigott05_100-0"><a href="#cite_note-Pigott05-100">[100]</a></sup> On the evening of 9 December 2010, the Prince of Wales and the <a href="/wiki/Camilla,_Duchess_of_Cornwall" title="Camilla, Duchess of Cornwall">Duchess of Cornwall</a> were travelling in the Silver Jubilee Car to the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Variety_Performance" title="Royal Variety Performance">Royal Variety Performance</a> in London when it was attacked by <a href="/wiki/2010_United_Kingdom_student_protests" title="2010 United Kingdom student protests">student protesters</a>; the couple were unhurt, but the car, which was not armoured, was spattered with paint and one of the side windows was smashed.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101"><a href="#cite_note-101">[101]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_vehicles_of_the_royal_family">Personal vehicles of the royal family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=115" title="Edit section: Personal vehicles of the royal family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>For non-official journeys, the Queen will usually be driven in a dark green <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Mulsanne_(2010)" title="Bentley Mulsanne (2010)">Bentley Mulsanne</a> or in an armoured <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_XJ" title="Jaguar XJ">Jaguar XJ</a>, similar to that used by the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister</a>. This is escorted by the same vehicles as a state car. She also occasionally uses a <a href="/wiki/Range_Rover" title="Range Rover">Range Rover</a>, particularly for visits to rural areas and events such as county shows. On visits to <a href="/wiki/Balmoral_Castle" title="Balmoral Castle">Balmoral</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sandringham_House" title="Sandringham House">Sandringham</a>, as portrayed in the film <i><a href="/wiki/The_Queen_(film)" title="The Queen (film)">The Queen</a></i>, she has been seen at the wheel of a <a href="/wiki/Land_Rover_Defender" title="Land Rover Defender">Land Rover Defender</a>. Her Majesty also owns a <a href="/wiki/Rover_P5" title="Rover P5">Rover P5</a>, which is on permanent display at the <a href="/wiki/British_Motor_Heritage" title="British Motor Heritage">British Motor Heritage</a> Centre, <a href="/wiki/Gaydon" title="Gaydon">Gaydon</a>. <a href="/wiki/Prince_Philip,_Duke_of_Edinburgh" title="Prince Philip, Duke of Edinburgh">The Duke of Edinburgh</a> owns a <a href="/wiki/Land_Rover_Discovery" title="Land Rover Discovery">Land Rover Discovery</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Land_Rover_Freelander" title="Land Rover Freelander">Land Rover Freelander</a> and a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MetroCab" title="MetroCab">MetroCab</a>, the last of which he uses for trips around central London. The Duke sometimes drives a Land Rover Discovery around <a href="/wiki/Windsor_Great_Park" title="Windsor Great Park">Windsor Great Park</a>. Other members of the Royal Family are usually driven in <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a> or Range Rover models.</p>
<p>The Prince of Wales uses an armoured <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Turbo_R" title="Bentley Turbo R">Bentley Turbo R</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Range_Rover" title="Range Rover">Range Rover</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_XJ" title="Jaguar XJ">Jaguar XJ</a> or an <a href="/wiki/Audi_A6" title="Audi A6">Audi A6</a>. He also has an <a href="/wiki/Aston_Martin_DB6" title="Aston Martin DB6">Aston Martin DB6</a> volante, and an <a href="/wiki/Aston_Martin_V8" title="Aston Martin V8">Aston Martin V8</a> converted to run on biofuel made from surplus local white wine. His Jaguars, Audi and Range Rover use biodiesel made from recycled cooking oil.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102"><a href="#cite_note-102">[102]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Anne,_Princess_Royal" title="Anne, Princess Royal">The Princess Royal</a> owns a <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Continental_Flying_Spur_(2005)" title="Bentley Continental Flying Spur (2005)">Bentley Continental Flying Spur</a> which she uses for official and private engagements.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103"><a href="#cite_note-103">[103]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Prince_Andrew,_Duke_of_York" title="Prince Andrew, Duke of York">The Duke of York</a> uses a 2008 <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Arnage" title="Bentley Arnage">Bentley Arnage</a> with a personalised number plate with the letters 'DOY'.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-thesun.co.uk_104-0"><a href="#cite_note-thesun.co.uk-104">[104]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="British_government">British government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=116" title="Edit section: British government">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pm_jag.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="683" data-file-width="1024" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Pm_jag.jpg/220px-Pm_jag.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Pm_jag.jpg/330px-Pm_jag.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Pm_jag.jpg/440px-Pm_jag.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Pm_jag.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
2010 Jaguar XJ Sentinel Prime Ministerial Car</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Prime_Ministerial_Car_(United_Kingdom)" title="Prime Ministerial Car (United Kingdom)">Prime Ministerial Car (United Kingdom)</a></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister of the United Kingdom</a> is usually driven in one of a fleet of armoured <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_XJ" title="Jaguar XJ">Jaguar XJ Sentinel</a> models, escorted by <a href="/wiki/Range_Rover" title="Range Rover">Range Rover</a> or <a href="/wiki/Land_Rover_Discovery" title="Land Rover Discovery">Land Rover Discovery</a> vehicles and police motorcycle outriders. <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> arrived at <a href="/wiki/10_Downing_Street" title="10 Downing Street">10 Downing Street</a> following his appointment in a silver 2010 X350 model, but took delivery of his new X351 on 13 May 2010.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105"><a href="#cite_note-105">[105]</a></sup></p>
<p>Since the early-1980s, when <a href="/wiki/Margaret_Thatcher" title="Margaret Thatcher">Margaret Thatcher</a> switched from the <a href="/wiki/Rover_Company" title="Rover Company">Rover</a> <a href="/wiki/Rover_P5" title="Rover P5">P5</a> models that had been in use since the 1960s, all Prime Ministerial cars have been from the Jaguar XJ range of the day, or its <a href="/wiki/Daimler_Company" title="Daimler Company">Daimler</a>-badged variant. For the first few months of his premiership in 2007, <a href="/wiki/Gordon_Brown" title="Gordon Brown">Gordon Brown</a> reverted to the previous Prime Ministerial car, a navy blue (X308) model purchased in 2000, before starting to use the silver model.</p>
<p>The 2000 model replaced a British racing green X300 model, built for <a href="/wiki/John_Major" title="John Major">John Major</a>, which gained international media attention when it bore Tony Blair to Buckingham Palace on the day after the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_general_election,_1997" title="United Kingdom general election, 1997">1997 general election</a>. A <a href="/wiki/British_racing_green" title="British racing green">British racing green</a> X308 took Gordon Brown to <a href="/wiki/Buckingham_Palace" title="Buckingham Palace">Buckingham Palace</a> on 6 April 2010 to request the dissolution of Parliament, but it was the 2000 model that took him on his last ride as Prime Minister.</p>
<p>All former prime ministers since 1975 have been provided with an armoured car, usually the same model as the current Prime Minister, along with police protection. As of 2014<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup> John Major, Tony Blair and Gordon Brown were provided with cars. Blair also bought his own bespoke BMW 7-Series.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106"><a href="#cite_note-106">[106]</a></sup></p>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_government" title="British government">British government</a> maintains the <a href="/wiki/Government_Car_and_Despatch_Agency" title="Government Car and Despatch Agency">Government Car and Despatch Agency</a> which provides transport for senior government officials. In December 2008, the service took delivery of a fleet of armoured <a href="/wiki/BMW" title="BMW">BMW</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BMW_7-Series" title="BMW 7-Series">760Li</a> models for use by senior dignitaries and visiting politicians.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107"><a href="#cite_note-107">[107]</a></sup> The service also uses vehicles from <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_Cars" title="Jaguar Cars">Jaguar</a>, Land Rover, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ford" title="Ford">Ford</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vauxhall_Motors" title="Vauxhall Motors">Vauxhall</a>, while some ministers use <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Prius" title="Toyota Prius">Toyota Prius</a> hybrid models.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="British_Virgin_Islands">British Virgin Islands</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=117" title="Edit section: British Virgin Islands">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The current <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Governor_of_the_British_Virgin_Islands" title="Governor of the British Virgin Islands">Governor of the British Virgin Islands</a> is driven in a grey Royal Service Range Rover from Great Britain with a license plate symbolizing the Crown. He is usually driven by a Police Officer from the RVIPF (Royal Virgin Islands Police Force).</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cayman_Islands">Cayman Islands</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=118" title="Edit section: Cayman Islands">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_the_Cayman_Islands" title="Governor of the Cayman Islands">Governor of the Cayman Islands</a> is driven in a beige <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cadillac_DeVille" title="Cadillac DeVille">Cadillac DeVille</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sedan_(car)" title="Sedan (car)">sedan</a>. Surmounted on the hood is the flag of the office, and instead of license plates the car has a crown on the front and back. It is likely that the car is armoured but this is not known for certain. Other senior officials and visiting VIPs use a fleet of armoured <a href="/wiki/Ford_Excursion" title="Ford Excursion">Ford Excursions</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="United_States_of_America">United States of America</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=119" title="Edit section: United States of America">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Presidential_state_car_(United_States)" title="Presidential state car (United States)">Presidential state car (United States)</a></div>
<p>The President of the United States travels in a heavily armored, custom-built limousine, which is often referred to as Limo One, Cadillac One, or its less formal nickname of "The Beast." The vehicle is based on a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/GMC_Topkick" title="GMC Topkick">GMC Topkick</a> platform, and has the outward appearance of an enlarged <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_DTS" title="Cadillac DTS">Cadillac DTS</a> limousine, with styling elements from other vehicles in the Cadillac lineup.</p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:227px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:GPA02-09_US_SecretService_press_release_2009_Limousine_Page_3_Image.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="872" data-file-width="1264" height="155" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/GPA02-09_US_SecretService_press_release_2009_Limousine_Page_3_Image.jpg/225px-GPA02-09_US_SecretService_press_release_2009_Limousine_Page_3_Image.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/GPA02-09_US_SecretService_press_release_2009_Limousine_Page_3_Image.jpg/338px-GPA02-09_US_SecretService_press_release_2009_Limousine_Page_3_Image.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/GPA02-09_US_SecretService_press_release_2009_Limousine_Page_3_Image.jpg/450px-GPA02-09_US_SecretService_press_release_2009_Limousine_Page_3_Image.jpg 2x" width="225"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:GPA02-09_US_SecretService_press_release_2009_Limousine_Page_3_Image.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
2009 Cadillac Presidential State Car, commonly referred to as Cadillac One.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The Cadillac One is a 2009 model year. The vehicle features bulletproof windows, state-of-the-art communication and protection systems, a stowable desk, and a gas-proof chamber for defense against gas attacks. However, there is a new limo in the works, most likely a stretched and armored Cadillac CT6 or Escalade, likely to debut in inauguration day 2017.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108"><a href="#cite_note-108">[108]</a></sup></p>
<p>On 24 May 2011, an earlier "Beast" failed to clear the driveway of the <a href="/wiki/Embassy_of_the_United_States,_Dublin" title="Embassy of the United States, Dublin">U.S. Embassy compound in Dublin, Ireland</a>. Though President <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> was the escorted official, he was in the second limo as the first noisily struck the pavement hump under the Embassy gate.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109"><a href="#cite_note-109">[109]</a></sup></p>
<p>Unlike most other <a href="/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">heads of state</a>, with the occasional exception of the <a href="/wiki/Monarchy_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Monarchy of the United Kingdom">British Monarch</a> and the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">President of Russia</a>, the U.S. President is accompanied on all foreign and domestic trips by a full motorcade of U.S. government vehicles, including several presidential limousines, escort vehicles and a military ambulance, all of which are transported by the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">United States Air Force</a> using <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/C-17_Globemaster_III" title="C-17 Globemaster III">C-17 Globemaster III</a> aircraft. The U.S. vehicles are typically complemented with coaches, police vehicles, ambulances and limousines provided by local authorities.</p>
<p>Members of Congress have an allowance of $1,000 per month in which the government may cover the cost of a lease, not including mobile offices. The preferred car for members of Congress was the <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Town_Car" title="Lincoln Town Car">Lincoln Town Car</a> until its discontinuation. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Executive_cars" title="Executive cars">Executive cars</a> are the most common type of car for Congressmen. The two most popular cars for Congressmen are the Town Car's successors: the <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_MKS" title="Lincoln MKS">MKS</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_MKT" title="Lincoln MKT">MKT</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110"><a href="#cite_note-110">[110]</a></sup> U.S. State Governors and Cabinet officials were often driven in a <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_DTS" title="Cadillac DTS">Cadillac DTS</a>, but the modern <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_XTS" title="Cadillac XTS">XTS</a> is now standard. Almost all senior officials use the <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Suburban" title="Chevrolet Suburban">Chevrolet Suburban</a> as an alternative form of transportation.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Puerto_Rico">Puerto Rico</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=120" title="Edit section: Puerto Rico">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Current Gov. <a href="/wiki/Alejandro_Garc%C3%ADa_Padilla" title="Alejandro García Padilla">Alejandro García Padilla</a> has chosen a black Chrysler 300<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111"><a href="#cite_note-111">[111]</a></sup> from his government's pool of vehicles confiscated from criminals and sold to the Governor's office for a nominal $2,000. The former <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Governor of Puerto Rico">Governor of Puerto Rico</a> used a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Tahoe_Hybrid" title="Chevrolet Tahoe Hybrid">Chevrolet Tahoe Hybrid</a>. <a href="/wiki/Ford_Expedition" title="Ford Expedition">Ford Expeditions</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Sequoia" title="Toyota Sequoia">Toyota Sequoias</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Nissan_Armada" title="Nissan Armada">Nissan Armadas</a> are available in the fleet from previous administrations. As part of the current Governor's motorcade, two large black SUVs, one white <a href="/wiki/Ford_Crown_Victoria" title="Ford Crown Victoria">Ford Crown Victorias</a> and at least one police motorcycle are used. They carry standard Puerto Rico license plates. Former Governor Luis Fortuño's specialty plate had the "LGF-051" numeration.</p>
<p>Governor <a href="/wiki/Luis_Mu%C3%B1oz_Mar%C3%ADn" title="Luis Muñoz Marín">Luis Muñoz Marín</a> (1949–1965) used an armored <a href="/wiki/Packard" title="Packard">Packard</a> given to him by President <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Harry_S_Truman" title="Harry S Truman">Harry S Truman</a>, which is on exhibition at the Muñoz Marín Foundation Library and Museum. Governor <a href="/wiki/Rafael_Hern%C3%A1ndez_Col%C3%B3n" title="Rafael Hernández Colón">Rafael Hernández Colón</a> (1973–1977, 1985–1993) ordered an armored <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ford" title="Ford">Ford</a> station wagon for which he was severely criticized and, thus, rarely used.</p>
<p>Each sitting Governor has the right to change the gubernatorial fleet as he or she may see fit, for example, <a href="/wiki/Pedro_Rossell%C3%B3" title="Pedro Rosselló">Pedro Rosselló</a> used a <a href="/wiki/Mercury_Grand_Marquis" title="Mercury Grand Marquis">Mercury Grand Marquis</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Tahoe" title="Chevrolet Tahoe">GMC Yukon</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sila_Calder%C3%B3n" title="Sila Calderón">Sila Calderón</a> used a <a href="/wiki/Ford_Expedition" title="Ford Expedition">Ford Expedition</a> and sometimes, for special occasions, a <a href="/wiki/Buick_Park_Avenue" title="Buick Park Avenue">Buick Park Avenue</a>, while <a href="/wiki/An%C3%ADbal_Acevedo_Vil%C3%A1" title="Aníbal Acevedo Vilá">Aníbal Acevedo Vilá</a> used Nissan Armadas. As a tradition <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Full_size_cars" title="Full size cars">full size cars</a> were used but since the late 1990s, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SUV" title="SUV">SUVs</a> are being used.</p>
<p>Former Governors are entitled to an official vehicle, which is replaced every four years throughout their life.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Uruguay">Uruguay</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=121" title="Edit section: Uruguay">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:1971_Volkswagen_Beetle_(Type_1)_sedan_(25123273943).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3168" data-file-width="4752" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/1971_Volkswagen_Beetle_%28Type_1%29_sedan_%2825123273943%29.jpg/220px-1971_Volkswagen_Beetle_%28Type_1%29_sedan_%2825123273943%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/1971_Volkswagen_Beetle_%28Type_1%29_sedan_%2825123273943%29.jpg/330px-1971_Volkswagen_Beetle_%28Type_1%29_sedan_%2825123273943%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/1971_Volkswagen_Beetle_%28Type_1%29_sedan_%2825123273943%29.jpg/440px-1971_Volkswagen_Beetle_%28Type_1%29_sedan_%2825123273943%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:1971_Volkswagen_Beetle_(Type_1)_sedan_(25123273943).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A Volkswagen Beetle similar to the one driven by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jose_Mujica" title="Jose Mujica">Jose Mujica</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The presidential state car of <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a> is an armoured 2005 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Vectra" title="Chevrolet Vectra">Chevrolet Vectra</a>, purchased by president <a href="/wiki/Tabar%C3%A9_V%C3%A1zquez" title="Tabaré Vázquez">Tabaré Vázquez</a> when his term in office began on March 1, 2005. Previously, the Uruguayan head of state traveled in a <a href="/wiki/Mitsubishi_Galant" title="Mitsubishi Galant">Mitsubishi Galant</a> procured from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Uruguay" title="Government of Uruguay">government</a>'s fleet of diplomatic vehicles.</p>
<p>As of August 2007, the presidential motor pool includes <a href="/wiki/Mitsubishi_Galant" title="Mitsubishi Galant">Mitsubishi Galants</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Corolla" title="Toyota Corolla">Toyota Corollas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Vento" title="Volkswagen Vento">Volkswagen Ventos</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Rover_75" title="Rover 75">Rover 75s</a>.</p>
<p>Municipal <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Intendants" title="Intendants">intendants</a> of Uruguay are transported in armored <a href="/wiki/Peugeot_607" title="Peugeot 607">Peugeot 607s</a>.</p>
<p>After 2010, the official state car was no longer used. President <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jose_Mujica" title="Jose Mujica">Jose Mujica</a> instead drives a <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen_Beetle" title="Volkswagen Beetle">Volkswagen Beetle</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112"><a href="#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Uzbekistan">Uzbekistan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=122" title="Edit section: Uzbekistan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The state limousines of Uzbekistan are two special ordered 2010 <a href="/wiki/Range_Rover" title="Range Rover">Range Rover</a> Supercharged with bulletproof windows. Also, the President of the Republic of Uzbekistan is transported by an armored Mercedes-Benz S-class which is escorted by other similar vehicles.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Vatican">Vatican</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=123" title="Edit section: Vatican">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Popemobile" title="Popemobile">Popemobile</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pope_Benedict_XVI_1_04062011.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1185" data-file-width="1091" height="239" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Pope_Benedict_XVI_1_04062011.JPG/220px-Pope_Benedict_XVI_1_04062011.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Pope_Benedict_XVI_1_04062011.JPG/330px-Pope_Benedict_XVI_1_04062011.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Pope_Benedict_XVI_1_04062011.JPG/440px-Pope_Benedict_XVI_1_04062011.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Pope_Benedict_XVI_1_04062011.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_M-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz M-Class">Mercedes-Benz M-Class</a> Popemobile</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The pope has several vehicles. Most famous is the custom-made white <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_M-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz M-Class">Mercedes-Benz M-Class</a> with an armoured glass compartment at the back. When the pope goes to the weekly audience at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saint_Peter%27s_Square" title="Saint Peter's Square">Saint Peter's Square</a> he uses a white open-top <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_G-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz G-Class">Mercedes-Benz G-Class</a>. There is also an armoured <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_S-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz S-Class">Mercedes-Benz S-Class</a> in the Vatican garage, and a custom-made <a href="/wiki/Lancia_Thesis" title="Lancia Thesis">Lancia Thesis</a>. All the <a href="/wiki/Popemobile" title="Popemobile">popemobiles</a> and limousines have registration SCV 1. In September 2012 the Pope received an electrical custom-made <a href="/wiki/Renault_Kangoo" title="Renault Kangoo">Renault Kangoo</a> for use around his Summer Residence <a href="/wiki/Castel_Gandolfo" title="Castel Gandolfo">Castel Gandolfo</a>. The mini-van is white with the pope's crest on the door. There is a second electrical Kangoo, delivered in blue, for the Vatican Police.</p>
<p>As of September 2013 <a href="/wiki/Pope_Francis" title="Pope Francis">Pope Francis</a> owns a 1984 <a href="/wiki/Renault_4" title="Renault 4">Renault 4</a>. It was given to him by its previous owner – Father Renzo Zocca, a priest in northern Italy. <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113"><a href="#cite_note-113">[113]</a></sup></p>
<p>In 2014, Pope Francis shunned the use of the armored vehicle and opted for open-air Popemobiles so he may get close to the people more. He used an open-air, custom-made Kia Popemobile during his apostolic visit to Korea. He also used the same Kia Popemobile and two (2) other glass-less Popemobiles during his visit in the Philippines in January 2015.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Venezuela">Venezuela</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=124" title="Edit section: Venezuela">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a>, president until his death in 2013, sometimes drove a red <a href="/wiki/IKCO_Samand" title="IKCO Samand">IKCO Samand</a> badged Centauro, or in red or green a <a href="/wiki/Tiuna" title="Tiuna">Tiuna</a> truck accompanied with some ministers or governors or mayors, depending on the occasion when he travelled, usually with a high security personnel around, with a large convoy of armored <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SUV" title="SUV">SUV</a> conformed by <a href="/wiki/Ford_Explorer" title="Ford Explorer">Ford Explorer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Suburban" title="Chevrolet Suburban">Chevrolet Suburban</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Tahoe" title="Chevrolet Tahoe">Chevrolet Tahoe</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Trailblazer" title="Chevrolet Trailblazer">Chevrolet Trailblazer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Express" title="Chevrolet Express">Chevrolet Express</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ford_Expedition" title="Ford Expedition">Ford Expedition</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_4Runner" title="Toyota 4Runner">Toyota 4Runner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Fortuner" title="Toyota Fortuner">Toyota Fortuner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Sequoia" title="Toyota Sequoia">Toyota Sequoia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jeep_Grand_Cherokee" title="Jeep Grand Cherokee">Jeep Grand Cherokee</a>, and an ambulance in case of any emergency, plus is escorted with the Presidential Guard that uses armored Toyota Land Cruiser (80&amp;90 Series), the transit police and the <a href="/wiki/Venezuelan_National_Guard" title="Venezuelan National Guard">Venezuelan National Guard</a> motorcycle officers have the duty to escort the motorcade and to clear up the traffic.</p>
<p>Another fleet of vehicles includes a <a href="/wiki/Cadillac_Fleetwood" title="Cadillac Fleetwood">Cadillac Fleetwood</a> that is used for national holidays like special parades, also the president used 3 armoured black <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_E-Class" title="Mercedes-Benz E-Class">(W211)</a>, these vehicles have license plates with the national emblem, but are used for special occasions or important meetings when <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> met with other presidents. Another vehicle is an armored silver <a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Town_Car" title="Lincoln Town Car">Lincoln Town Car</a> used to transport the president's visitors from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sim%C3%B3n_Bol%C3%ADvar_International_Airport_of_Maiquetia" title="Simón Bolívar International Airport of Maiquetia">Simón Bolívar International Airport of Maiquetia</a> to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palacio_de_Miraflores" title="Palacio de Miraflores">Palacio de Miraflores</a> and back.</p>
<p>The vice president is usually driven in an armored <a href="/wiki/Nissan_Patrol" title="Nissan Patrol">Nissan Patrol</a> with a motorcade of 4 or 5 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SUV" title="SUV">SUV</a>. Ministers usually travel in armored vehicles including <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Impala" title="Chevrolet Impala">Chevrolet Impala</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Trailblazer" title="Chevrolet Trailblazer">Chevrolet Trailblazer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet_Tahoe" title="Chevrolet Tahoe">Chevrolet Tahoe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jeep_Grand_Cherokee" title="Jeep Grand Cherokee">Jeep Grand Cherokee</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_4Runner" title="Toyota 4Runner">Toyota 4Runner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Camry" title="Toyota Camry">Toyota Camry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Fortuner" title="Toyota Fortuner">Toyota Fortuner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ford_Fusion_(Americas)" title="Ford Fusion (Americas)">Ford Fusion (Americas)</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ford_Explorer" title="Ford Explorer">Ford Explorer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ford_Expedition" title="Ford Expedition">Ford Expedition</a>, also escorted by <a href="/wiki/Venezuelan_National_Guard" title="Venezuelan National Guard">Venezuelan National Guard</a> officers.</p>
<p>The last acquisition to the fleet is a <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Continental_Flying_Spur_(2005)" title="Bentley Continental Flying Spur (2005)">Bentley Continental Flying Spur</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114"><a href="#cite_note-114">[114]</a></sup></p>
<p>President <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nicolas_Maduro" title="Nicolas Maduro">Nicolas Maduro</a> is driving a black <a href="/wiki/Toyota_4Runner" title="Toyota 4Runner">Toyota 4Runner</a> or a <a href="/wiki/Ford_Explorer" title="Ford Explorer">Ford Explorer</a> often accompanied with the Venezuela Presidential Honor Guard motorcade with his assistants and ministers.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Vietnam">Vietnam</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=125" title="Edit section: Vietnam">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The President of Vietnam is driven in a <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Continental_Flying_Spur" title="Bentley Continental Flying Spur">Bentley Continental Flying Spur</a> Speed.The Presidential Household has also two <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W221" title="Mercedes-Benz W221">Mercedes-Benz S600 Pullman</a> W221. Ministers usually travel in Mercedes-Benz S500, E500, Porsche Cayenne, Cadillac Escalade and <a href="/wiki/BMW_7_Series" title="BMW 7 Series">BMW 7 Series</a> <a href="/wiki/Limousine" title="Limousine">limousine</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lexus_LS_(XF40)#LS_600h" title="Lexus LS (XF40)">Lexus LS 600h L</a> . The Prime Minister use the new Mercedes-Benz S500 W222, all government cars have blue licences plates but some have white civil licence plate with a government placard behind the windshield.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Yugoslavia">Yugoslavia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=126" title="Edit section: Yugoslavia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>President <a href="/wiki/Josip_Broz_Tito" title="Josip Broz Tito">Josip Broz Tito</a>, used a custom-built <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_600" title="Mercedes-Benz 600">Mercedes-Benz 600</a> limo with removable top for most functions. Tito also had several luxury cars in his private motor pool collection, including: numerous <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes_Benz" title="Mercedes Benz">Mercedes Benz</a> models, including a <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_540K" title="Mercedes-Benz 540K">540k</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_770" title="Mercedes-Benz 770">770k</a> seized from <a href="/wiki/Ante_Paveli%C4%87" title="Ante Pavelić">Ante Pavelić</a> after WWII, a <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Phantom_V" title="Rolls-Royce Phantom V">Rolls-Royce Phantom V</a>, and several <a href="/wiki/Cadillac" title="Cadillac">Cadillac</a> and <a href="/wiki/Chevrolet" title="Chevrolet">Chevrolet</a> models.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115"><a href="#cite_note-115">[115]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Zambia">Zambia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Official_state_car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=127" title="Edit section: Zambia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As of July 2011 the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_Zambia" title="President of Zambia">President of Zambia</a> was driven in an armoured <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_W221" title="Mercedes-Benz W221">Mercedes-Benz S600 Pullman</a> limousine, escorted by 30 officers of the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Zambia_Police&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Zambia Police (page does not exist)">Zambia Police</a> trained in diplomatic protection on <a href="/wiki/BMW" title="BMW">BMW</a> motorcycles and in six <a href="/wiki/BMW_3_Series" title="BMW 3 Series">BMW 3 Series</a> E93 cars. His motorcade also includes an ambulance at all times. For visits to rural areas the president uses an armoured Toyota Land Cruiser 100 Series.</p>
